Explore full API workflows, test calls, and view sample payloads.

Transaction Token Lifecycle (Interactive Recipe)

Step through the complete transaction token flow—from creation and payment to verification, refunds, updates, and cancellation—using an interactive, copy-ready walkthrough with real request and response examples.

Key Transaction Flows

Below is a structured mapping of the core operations within this section.

Create Token
Initiate a payment and receive a secure token.

Payment Result Callbacks
Receive notifications for approved, declined, or failed payments.

Transaction Status Lookup
Verify transaction status if callbacks are missed.

Refund / Void
Reverse or refund a completed payment.

Customer Checkout Redirect
Redirect the shopper to DPO’s Hosted Payment Page.

Email Payment Link
Generate payment links via email.

Verify xPay
Validate xPay transactions securely.

mVISA QR Code
Create QR-based payment requests.

When to Use Transaction Operations

Use this section when you need to:

Build an end-to-end online checkout

Integrate DPO Pay into your e-commerce experience

Support hosted and non-hosted payment flows

Handle asynchronous callbacks reliably

Automate refunds, reversals, and payout operations

Provide alternative checkout methods such as QR and xPay

If you're integrating for the first time, begin with Create Token → Redirect → Callback, then expand into more advanced operations as your use case grows.

Create Token  
============  
 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

The `createToken` request is the first step in creating a payment with DPO Pay by Network. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

createToken (v6)  
----------------  
 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

The `createToken` operation is the first step in initiating a payment with DPO Pay by Network. It generates a secure payment token that represents a single checkout session. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

You’ll use this token to:  
-  Redirect the customer to the hosted DPO checkout page, or  
-  Continue processing flows such as status checks or refunds. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Legacy note: Some fields and endpoints may still reference “3G Direct Pay” (`3G`). This is the same platform, now branded as DPO Pay by Network. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Endpoint  
--------  
 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Method: `POST`  
Headers:  
`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

POST URL:  
`https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

DPO does not provide a separate sandbox. Test credentials are issued on this endpoint and later promoted to live mode. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Required XML Fields  
-------------------  
 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Field | Description  
----- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Merchant token assigned by DPO  
`Request` | Must be `createToken`  
`PaymentAmount` | Amount (e.g., `450.00`)  
`PaymentCurrency` | ISO currency (e.g., `ZAR`)  
`CompanyRef` | Your order reference  
`RedirectURL` | Where the customer is sent after payment  
`BackURL` | Server callback URL for final status  
`ServiceType` | Provided by DPO during merchant onboarding  
`Description` | Payment description  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Optional customer fields improve receipts and reporting: `customerFirstName`, `customerLastName`, `customerEmail`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Example Request (XML)  
---------------------  
 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Replace values with your own `CompanyToken`, URLs, and `ServiceType`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Example structure:  
-  XML declaration with version and encoding  
-  Root element containing:  
  – `CompanyToken`  
  – `Request` = `createToken`  
  – `PaymentAmount`  
  – `PaymentCurrency`  
  – `CompanyRef`  
  – `RedirectURL`  
  – `BackURL`  
  – `PTL` (Payment Time Limit)  
  – `ServiceType`  
  – Customer details (first name, last name, email)  
  – Additional booking fields such as route, description, and travel date/time as per your business case. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

PTL refers to the Payment Time Limit in hours (how long the payment token stays active before expiring); the default varies by merchant account. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Example Success Response (XML)  
------------------------------  
 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

A typical successful response contains:  
-  `Result` = `000` (success)  
-  `ResultExplanation` = `Transaction created`  
-  `TransToken` = token used to redirect the customer  
-  `TransRef` = DPO transaction reference. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

You then redirect the customer to:  
`https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/pay.asp?ID={TransToken}` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Example Error Response  
----------------------  
 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Example structure:  
-  `Result` = error code (e.g., `904`)  
-  `ResultExplanation` = error description (e.g., `Invalid currency code`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

For the full list of error and gateway result codes, see Gateway Response Codes (v6). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Payment Flow Summary  
--------------------  
 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

High-level flow:  
1. Merchant Server → DPO API: POST `createToken`  
2. DPO API → Merchant Server: returns `TransToken` with `Result` = `000`  
3. Customer → DPO: browser is redirected to DPO checkout using `TransToken`  
4. DPO → Merchant Server: sends callback to `BackURL` with final result  
5. Merchant (optional) → DPO API: calls `verifyToken` to confirm transaction status. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Going Live Checklist  
--------------------  
 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Item | Done  
---- | ----  
Use test credentials issued by DPO | ☐  
Switch same credentials to live when approved | ☐  
HTTPS on `RedirectURL` and `BackURL` | ☐  
Return `HTTP 200 OK` to callbacks | ☐  
Log `TransToken`, `TransRef`, `CompanyRef`, `Result` | ☐  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Branding note: You may still see “3G” in examples; internally this is the same platform. Use “DPO Pay by Network” in your merchant-facing integrations. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/create-token)

Here is the full content of the “Payment Result Callbacks” page, cleaned and ready to paste into a `.txt` file. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/payment-result-callbacks)

Payment Result Callbacks

After a payment is completed, DPO Pay by Network sends the final result back to your system.

createToken (v6)

The `createToken` operation is the first step in initiating a payment with DPO Pay by Network. It generates a secure payment token that represents a single checkout session.

You’ll use this token to:
- Redirect the customer to the hosted DPO checkout page, or
- Continue processing flows such as status checks or refunds.

Legacy note: Some fields and endpoints may still reference “3G Direct Pay” (`3G`). This is the same platform, now branded as DPO Pay by Network.

Endpoint

Method: POST

Headers:
Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8
Accept: application/xml

POST URL:
https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/

DPO does not provide a public sandbox environment. To request test credentials, contact the Network International sales team at talktous@network.global.

A Postman collection link is also provided on the page.

Required XML Fields

Field | Description
------|------------
CompanyToken | Merchant token assigned by DPO
Request | Must be `createToken`
PaymentAmount | Amount (e.g., `450.00`)
PaymentCurrency | ISO currency (e.g., `ZAR`)
CompanyRef | Your order reference
RedirectURL | Where the customer is sent after payment
BackURL | Server callback URL for final status
ServiceType | Provided by DPO during merchant onboarding
Description | Payment description

Optional customer fields improve receipts and reporting:
- `customerFirstName`
- `customerLastName`
- `customerEmail`

Example Request (XML)

Replace values with your own `CompanyToken`, URLs, and `ServiceType`.

Example structure:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>8D3DA73D-9D7F-4E09-96D4-3D44E7A83EA3</CompanyToken>
  <Request>createToken</Request>
  <PaymentAmount>450.00</PaymentAmount>
  <PaymentCurrency>ZAR</PaymentCurrency>
  <CompanyRef>49FKEOA</CompanyRef>
  <RedirectURL>https://www.domain.com/payurl.php</RedirectURL>
  <BackURL>https://www.domain.com/backurl.php</BackURL>
  <PTL>0</PTL>
  <ServiceType>5</ServiceType>
  <customerFirstName>Alex</customerFirstName>
  <customerLastName>Nkosi</customerLastName>
  <customerEmail>customer@example.com</customerEmail>
  <Booking>
    <BookingRef>3854</BookingRef>
    <Description>Flight from Nairobi to Diani</Description>
    <Date>2025/12/20 19:00</Date>
  </Booking>
</API3G>

PTL refers to the Payment Time Limit in hours (how long the payment token stays active before expiring). The default value varies by merchant account.

Example Success Response (XML)

This is the example success response shown:

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transaction created</ResultExplanation>
  <TransToken>1B454D71-23EB-42E9-8FE8-FDDC167B5BCD</TransToken>
  <TransRef>R73770389</TransRef>
</API3G>

Field meanings:

Field | Meaning
------|--------
Result = 000 | Success
TransToken | Token used to redirect the customer
TransRef | DPO transaction reference

Redirect the customer here:

https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/pay.asp?ID=1B454D71-23EB-42E9-8FE8-FDDC167B5BCD

Example Error Response

Example error response:

<API3G>
  <Result>904</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Invalid currency code</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>

For the full list of result codes, see:
Gateway Response Codes (v6)

Payment Flow Summary

High-level payment flow:

1. Merchant Server → DPO API: POST `createToken`
2. DPO API → Merchant Server: return `TransToken` with `Result = 000`
3. Customer → DPO: browser is redirected to DPO checkout using `TransToken`
4. DPO → Merchant Server: DPO calls the configured `BackURL` with the final result
5. Merchant Server (optional) → DPO API: call `verifyToken` to confirm transaction status

Push Payments Callback

DPO may send automatic server-to-server notifications to a configured endpoint after a successful payment.

This push notification mechanism allows merchants to receive payment confirmation without relying on browser redirects.

For full details, see:
Push Payments Callback

Going Live Checklist

Item | Done
-----|-----
Use test credentials issued by DPO | ☐
Switch same credentials to live when approved | ☐
HTTPS on `RedirectURL` and `BackURL` | ☐
Return `HTTP 200 OK` to callbacks | ☐
Log `TransToken`, `TransRef`, `CompanyRef`, `Result` | ☐

Branding Note

You may still see “3G” in examples — internally this is the same platform. Use “DPO Pay by Network” in your merchant-facing integrations.

Push Payments Callback

DPO may send automatic server-to-server notifications to a configured endpoint after a successful payment. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

This push notification mechanism allows merchants to receive payment confirmation without relying on browser redirects or client-side actions. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Overview

The Push Payments Callback (`pushPayments`) is a server-to-server notification sent by DPO to the merchant’s backend system when a payment has been successfully processed. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

This ensures reliable transaction confirmation even if: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

- The customer closes the browser  
- The redirect flow fails  
- Network issues interrupt the checkout process  
- The payment occurs on a different device [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Merchants should treat this notification as the authoritative payment result. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

When is the callback sent?

The `pushPayments` notification is sent: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

- After a successful payment authorisation  
- To the callback URL configured for your merchant account  
- Independently of any customer redirect flow [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Note: The notification is not triggered for failed or cancelled payments unless specifically configured. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Endpoint requirements

Your system must expose a publicly accessible HTTPS endpoint capable of receiving HTTP POST requests from DPO. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Requirements

- Must support HTTPS  
- Must accept POST requests  
- Should respond quickly (recommended under 5 seconds)  
- Must return a valid HTTP 200 response to acknowledge receipt [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Failure to respond correctly may result in retries or missed confirmations. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Request format

The callback is sent as a POST request containing transaction details in the request body. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Typical information includes: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

- Merchant reference / order ID  
- Transaction ID  
- Payment status  
- Amount  
- Currency  
- Payment method  
- Timestamp [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

The exact fields may vary depending on your integration and configuration. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Example callback payload

JSON: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

```json
{
  "transactionId": "123456789",
  "merchantOrderId": "ORDER_12345",
  "status": "SUCCESS",
  "amount": 1000,
  "currency": "ZAR",
  "paymentMethod": "CARD",
  "timestamp": "2026-02-17T08:45:12Z"
}
```


Handling the callback

Upon receiving the notification, your system should: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

1. Validate the request source (if IP allowlisting or signatures are used)  
2. Verify the transaction details against your records  
3. Update the order status in your system  
4. Trigger fulfilment processes if applicable  
5. Return an HTTP 200 OK response [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Do not rely solely on browser redirects for payment confirmation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Recommended verification step

For critical operations, merchants should confirm the transaction status using the Transaction Status Lookup API before fulfilling the order. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

This protects against: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

- Duplicate notifications  
- Tampered requests  
- Network retries  
- Edge-case failures [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Idempotency considerations

Your system should handle duplicate notifications safely. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Implement idempotent processing using the transaction ID or merchant order ID to ensure that repeated callbacks do not result in duplicate fulfilment. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Security considerations

To protect your system: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

- Validate incoming requests from trusted sources  
- Implement IP allowlisting if provided by DPO  
- Use HTTPS only  
- Avoid exposing internal systems directly  
- Log callback activity for audit purposes [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Contact DPO support for recommended security configurations. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Failure handling

If your endpoint does not respond successfully: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

- DPO may retry delivery (depending on configuration)  
- The transaction will still be considered successful on DPO’s side  
- Merchants should reconcile transactions using status lookup tools [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Related documentation

- Payment Result Callbacks  
- Transaction Status Lookup  
- Basic Transaction Operations [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/pushpayments)

Transaction Status Lookup

Use the Transaction Status Lookup operation to check the latest status of a transaction previously created with `createToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

createToken (v6)

The `createToken` operation is the first step in initiating a payment with DPO Pay by Network. It generates a secure payment token that represents a single checkout session. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

You’ll use this token to:  
- Redirect the customer to the hosted DPO checkout page, or  
- Continue processing flows such as status checks or refunds. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Legacy note: Some fields and endpoints may still reference 3G Direct Pay (`3G`). This is the same platform, now branded as DPO Pay by Network. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Endpoint

Method: `POST` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Headers:  
`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

POST URL:  
`https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

DPO does not provide a separate sandbox. Test credentials are issued on this endpoint and later promoted to live mode. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

(“Test in Postman” link is also provided on the page.) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Required XML Fields

Field | Description  
------|------------  
`CompanyToken` | Merchant token assigned by DPO  
`Request` | Must be `createToken`  
`PaymentAmount` | Amount (e.g., `450.00`)  
`PaymentCurrency` | ISO currency (e.g., `ZAR`)  
`CompanyRef` | Your order reference  
`RedirectURL` | Where the customer is sent after payment  
`BackURL` | Server callback URL for final status  
`ServiceType` | Provided by DPO during merchant onboarding  
`Description` | Payment description  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Optional customer fields improve receipts & reporting:  
`customerFirstName`, `customerLastName`, `customerEmail`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Example Request (XML)

Replace values with your own `CompanyToken`, URLs, and `ServiceType`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

XML structure shown on the page:

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>8D3DA73D-9D7F-4E09-96D4-3D44E7A83EA3</CompanyToken>
  <Request>createToken</Request>
  <PaymentAmount>450.00</PaymentAmount>
  <PaymentCurrency>ZAR</PaymentCurrency>
  <CompanyRef>49FKEOA</CompanyRef>
  <RedirectURL>https://www.domain.com/payurl.php</RedirectURL>
  <BackURL>https://www.domain.com/backurl.php</BackURL>
  <PTL>0</PTL>
  <ServiceType>5</ServiceType>
  <customerFirstName>Alex</customerFirstName>
  <customerLastName>Nkosi</customerLastName>
  <customerEmail>customer@example.com</customerEmail>
  <Booking>
    <BookingRef>3854</BookingRef>
    <Description>Flight from Nairobi to Diani</Description>
    <Date>2025/12/20 19:00</Date>
  </Booking>
</API3G>
``` 

PTL refers to the Payment Time Limit in hours (how long the payment token stays active before expiring). Default varies by merchant account. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Example Success Response (XML)

The page shows a working sample response: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transaction created</ResultExplanation>
  <TransToken>1B454D71-23EB-42E9-8FE8-FDDC167B5BCD</TransToken>
  <TransRef>R73770389</TransRef>
</API3G>
``` 

Field meanings: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Field | Meaning  
------|--------  
`Result = 000` | Success  
`TransToken` | Token used to redirect customer  
`TransRef` | DPO transaction reference  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Redirect the customer here: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

`https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/pay.asp?ID=1B454D71-23EB-42E9-8FE8-FDDC167B5BCD` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Example Error Response

```xml
<API3G>
  <Result>904</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Invalid currency code</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
``` 

See full list: Gateway Response Codes (v6). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

(Another “Test in Postman” link is provided.) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Payment Flow Summary

High-level flow summary on the page: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

1. Merchant Server → DPO API: POST `createToken`  
2. DPO API → Merchant Server: return `TransToken` with `Result = 000`  
3. Customer → DPO: redirect to DPO checkout using `TransToken`  
4. DPO → Merchant Server: BackURL callback with result  
5. Merchant Server (optional) → DPO API: `verifyToken` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Going Live Checklist

Item | Done  
-----|-----  
Use test credentials issued by DPO | ☐  
Switch same credentials to live when approved | ☐  
HTTPS on `RedirectURL` and `BackURL` | ☐  
Return `HTTP 200 OK` to callbacks | ☐  
Log `TransToken`, `TransRef`, `CompanyRef`, `Result` | ☐  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Branding Note

You may still see `3G` in examples — internally this is the same platform. Use DPO Pay by Network in your merchant-facing integrations. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-status-lookup)

Refund / Void (v6)

Use this operation to reverse a payment processed via DPO Pay by Network. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

DPO Pay supports two types of reversals: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Action | Meaning  
------|--------  
Void | Cancel an authorization or same-day sale before settlement  
Refund | Return funds after settlement (full or partial)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Always run a Transaction Status Lookup first to confirm whether the transaction has settled. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Endpoint [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/ [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Headers [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8  
Accept: application/xml [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Field | Description  
-----|------------  
CompanyToken | Your merchant token  
Request | refundToken or cancelToken  
TransactionToken | Transaction token  
refundAmount | Optional — send only for partial refunds  
refundDetails | Refund description or reason  
refundRef | Refund reference  
refundApproval | If sent, the refund will be verified by an inspector  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Minimum required: CompanyToken, Request, and TransactionToken. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Example — Partial Refund [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Request>refundToken</Request>
  <CompanyToken>8D3DA73D-9D7F-4E09-96D4-3D44E7A83EA3</CompanyToken>
  <TransactionToken>705F5049-5B38-49AB-895E-B6EE499AA3F0</TransactionToken>
  <refundAmount>1.2</refundAmount>
  <refundDetails>Item out of stock</refundDetails>
</API3G>
``` 

Example Response (Refund) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Refund successful</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
``` 

Example — Void (Cancel) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>8D3DA73D-9D7F-4E09-96D4-3D44E7A83EA3</CompanyToken>
  <Request>cancelToken</Request>
  <TransactionToken>CDE7067F-953D-475D-B3AD-9E412E4C4185</TransactionToken>
</API3G>
``` 

Example Response (Void) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Token been updated to status cancelled</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
``` 

Error Response [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>999</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Cant modify token status due to current status: Paid</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
``` 

Common Codes [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Code | Action  
----|--------  
000 | Token been updated to status cancelled  
999 | Custom error message  
804 | Error in XML  
950 | Request missing transaction level mandatory fields  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

See also: Verify Token Response Codes and Gateway Response Codes for full status tables. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Business Rules [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

- Void = before settlement (same business day)  
- Refund = after settlement  
- Partial refunds supported (until full value reversed)  
- Currency must match the original transaction [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Flow [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

1. Merchant → DPO API: refund/void XML request  
2. DPO API → Merchant: Result = 000 or error  
3. Merchant (optional) → DPO API: verifyToken  
4. Merchant: update order & finance logs [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Implementation Tips [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

- Prefer TransRef when possible  
- Always log: TransRef, Amount, Result, Reason  
- Handle retries gracefully to avoid double-refunds  
- Show friendly UI messages instead of raw codes [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Quick Developer Actions [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

The page provides example CTAs (links) for: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

- Verify Transaction (link to Transaction Status Lookup)  
- Response Codes (link to Gateway Response Codes) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Updated: about 2 months ago [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Next: Update Token [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/refund-void)

Update Token

Use `updateToken` to modify a **pending** payment before the shopper pays on the hosted checkout page.

Typical edits include: amount, description, PTL (expiry), customer details, Redirect/Back URLs, or service info.

You can only update a token **that hasn’t been paid or expired**.

DPO PAY API (V7)  
- DPO Pay API Collection (v7)

Powered by ReadMe

***

Endpoint

HTTP:  
POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/

Headers:

Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8  
Accept: application/xml

Required / Optional Fields

Only include the fields you want to change. Omitted fields remain as originally set.

Field | Type | Required | Description  
----- | ---- | -------- | -----------  
Request | string | Yes | Must be `updateToken`.  
CompanyToken | string | Yes | Token provided by 3G (DPO) to operate this API.  
TransactionToken | string | Yes | Transaction token from the `createToken` operation.  
PaymentAmount | number | No | Transaction amount (up to 2 decimal places).  
CompanyRef | string | No | Company reference number.  
CustomerEmail | string | No | Customer’s email address.  
CustomerFirstName | string | No | Customer’s first name.  
CustomerLastName | string | No | Customer’s last name.  
CustomerAddress | string | No | Customer’s address.  
CustomerCity | string | No | Customer’s city.  
CustomerCountry | string | No | ISO 3166-1 alpha-2 country code.  
CustomerDialCode | string | No | Country dial code (ISO 3166-1 alpha-2 reference).  
CustomerPhone | integer | No | Customer’s phone number.  
CustomerZip | string | No | Customer’s ZIP/postal code.  
CompanyAccRef | string | No | Internal accounting reference number.  
UserToken | string | No | Identifies the user who created the transaction.

Example Update Request (XML)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>8D3DA73D-9D7F-4E09-96D4-3D44E7A83EA3</CompanyToken>
  <Request>updateToken</Request>
  <TransactionToken>8C7E2A48-859E-4735-8B36-8B3358BAAAFF</TransactionToken>
  <PaymentAmount>44</PaymentAmount>
  <CompanyRef>DPO1212</CompanyRef>
  <CustomerEmail>test@directpay.online</CustomerEmail>
  <CustomerFirstName>Steven</CustomerFirstName>
  <CustomerLastName>Muallem</CustomerLastName>
  <CustomerAddress>Rose Avenue 6</CustomerAddress>
  <CustomerCity>Nairobi</CustomerCity>
  <CustomerCountry>KE</CustomerCountry>
  <CustomerDialCode>KE</CustomerDialCode>
  <CustomerPhone>4433332312</CustomerPhone>
  <CustomerZip>121212</CustomerZip>
  <CompanyAccRef>DPO3232</CompanyAccRef>
  <UserToken>DPO3232</UserToken>
</API3G>
```

Success Response

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Token been updated</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

Error Responses (examples)

Example 1 – token expired:

```xml
<API3G>
  <Result>903</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Payment time limit exceeded (token expired)</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

Example 2 – already cancelled or paid:

```xml
<API3G>
<API3G>
  <Result>904</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transaction already cancelled or paid</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

See also “Gateway Response Codes” and “Verify Token Response Codes” for full code tables.

Test in Postman

A “Test in Postman” link is provided on the page.

Rules & Constraints

- Token must be **unpaid** and **not expired** (`PTL` not elapsed).  
- Currency and amount must be valid for the merchant account.  
- Some merchants enforce `CompanyRef` uniqueness; respect your setting.  
- If the shopper already opened the checkout, refreshing the page will reflect changes.

Typical Flow

1. Merchant calls `createToken` and receives `TransToken`.  
2. (Optional) Merchant calls `updateToken` to adjust amount or customer details.  
3. Customer is redirected to the hosted checkout using the same `TransToken`.  
4. Customer completes payment.  
5. DPO sends BackURL callback with the result.

Implementation Tips

- Keep updates **idempotent** in your system (log every change against the token).  
- If you extend `PTL`, reflect this in your UI (e.g., update countdown timers).  
- After updating, you do **not** get a new token — you keep the same `TransToken`.  
- If `updateToken` fails due to expiry or paid state, create a new token and restart the flow.

Customer Checkout Redirect (Hosted Page)

Once you have a valid payment token from `createToken`, redirect your customer to the **DPO Hosted Checkout page** to complete payment securely. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

DPO Pay handles card entry, security checks, 3-D Secure, fraud logic, and transaction authorization. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

Redirect URL Format

Use this URL pattern: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

`https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/pay.asp?ID={TransToken}` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

Replace `{TransToken}` with the token returned from the `createToken` API. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

Example Redirect (HTML Button)

Example HTML anchor button pointing to the hosted checkout: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

```html
<a
  href="https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/pay.asp?ID=1B454D71-23EB-42E9-8FE8-FDDC167B5BCD"
  class="btn btn-primary"
>
  Proceed to Payment
</a>
```


Example button text: “🛒 Proceed to Payment”. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

PHP Redirect

Server-side redirect using PHP: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

```php
header("Location: https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/pay.asp?ID=" . $transToken);
exit;
```


Node.js / Express Redirect

Server-side redirect using Node.js / Express: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

```javascript
res.redirect("https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/pay.asp?ID=" + transToken);
```


Optional: Embedded Checkout (iframe)

Use this only if your UX requires inline checkout. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

DPO still hosts card entry (PCI safe); you are only embedding the hosted page in your site. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

Example iframe: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

```html
<iframe
  src="https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/pay.asp?ID=1B454D71-23EB-42E9-8FE8-FDDC167B5BCD"
  width="100%"
  height="650"
  frameborder="0"
  scrolling="yes"
></iframe>
```


Payment Flow

High-level sequence: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

1. Merchant site displays a checkout / “Pay” button.  
2. Customer clicks the button.  
3. Merchant redirects the browser to the DPO Hosted Checkout URL using `TransToken`.  
4. Customer completes payment on DPO’s hosted page.  
5. DPO sends a **BackURL callback** (server-to-server) to the merchant with the final result.  
6. DPO redirects the customer’s browser to the configured `RedirectURL` (cosmetic return page). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

The BackURL callback is the source of truth for final payment status; the browser redirect is for customer UX. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

Best Practices

- Use a **loading screen** while redirecting the customer to DPO.  
- Store `TransToken` and `CompanyRef` in your database before redirect.  
- Treat the **BackURL webhook** as the authoritative result.  
- Do not rely solely on browser redirects for order fulfilment. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

Next Steps

After redirect and payment completion, common needs and where to handle them: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

Need | Link  
---- | ----  
Receive payment result | Payment Callbacks  
Display order summary | Merchant UX  
Check final status | Status Lookup  
Handle refunds/voids | Refund & Void  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/customer-checkout-redirect-hosted-page)

Email Payment Link

Use `emailToToken` to instruct DPO to send a payment email for a token you already created with `createToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Email Payment Link for an Existing Token (`emailToToken`, v6) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

This operation does not create a token. It uses your existing `TransactionToken` (a.k.a. `TransToken`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Endpoint & Headers [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/`  

Headers  
`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Request [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Field | Required | Description  
----- | -------- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `emailToToken`  
`TransactionToken` | Yes | The token returned by `createToken`  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

If the token doesn’t already have a customer email attached, first call `updateToken` to add `customerEmail` (and optional phone/country), then call `emailToToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>emailToToken</Request>
  <TransactionToken>EC9E975A-A7A2-4031-8972-BF123CDD9EDD</TransactionToken>
</API3G>
```


Responses [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Implementations vary slightly by tenant. You’ll receive a high-level `Result` plus optional delivery details. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Example Success (email queued/sent) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Email queued</ResultExplanation>
  <TransactionToken>EC9E975A-A7A2-4031-8972-BF123CDD9EDD</TransactionToken>
</API3G>
```


Example “Not sent” (common on test tenants) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>001</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Check details</ResultExplanation>
  <ResultDetails>
    <Code>200</Code>
    <Description>Not sent</Description>
    <Code>200</Code>
    <Description>Not sent</Description>
  </ResultDetails>
</API3G>
```


Why you might see “Not sent”: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

- Outbound email/SMS is disabled for your merchant (very common in test)  
- Email templates/sender not configured on DPO’s side  
- No `customerEmail` associated with the token (add via `updateToken` first) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Test in Postman: a Postman link is provided on the page. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Delivery Troubleshooting [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

1. Ensure the token has an email. If not, update first: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>updateToken</Request>
  <TransactionToken>EC9E975A-A7A2-4031-8972-BF123CDD9EDD</TransactionToken>
  <CustomerFirstName>Alex</CustomerFirstName>
  <CustomerLastName>Nkosi</CustomerLastName>
  <CustomerEmail>customer@example.com</CustomerEmail>
</API3G>
```


2. If DPO delivery is disabled in test, send your own email with the hosted link: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

`https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/pay.asp?ID={TransToken}` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

3. Need DPO to send the messages from test? Ask DPO Support to enable email/SMS notifications and configure templates/sender for your merchant. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Typical Flow [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

1. Merchant calls `createToken` → gets `TransToken`.  
2. (Optional) Merchant calls `updateToken` to add `customerEmail`.  
3. Merchant calls `emailToToken` with `TransactionToken`.  
4. DPO sends email with pay link (if enabled).  
5. Customer opens link and pays on hosted page.  
6. DPO sends BackURL callback (final result).  
7. (Optional) Merchant calls `verifyToken` for reconciliation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Notes & Best Practices [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

- `emailToToken` does not modify token data; it only triggers the send. Use `updateToken` to attach/modify `customerEmail`, `customerPhone`, `PTL`, etc.  
- If you need a guaranteed experience, send your own email containing the hosted URL; the payment flow is identical.  
- Log: `TransToken`, `CompanyRef`, `Result`, and (if present) the `ResultDetails` delivery info. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Updated: about 2 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Next: Verify xPay [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-operations-email-payment-link)

Here’s the full “Verify xPay” page content, cleaned for a `.txt` document. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

***

Verify xPay

Use `verifyXpay` to retrieve the current status and details of an xPay allocation (money transferred between DPO merchant accounts). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Request returns xPay information. Typical use cases: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

- Reconciling internal transfers  
- Confirming an allocation’s status  
- Surfacing sender/receiver details in your back office [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Navigation / Context

- Getting Started with DPO Pay by Network  
- Basic Transaction Operations  
  - Overview  
  - Create Token  
  - Payment Result Callbacks  
    - Push Payments Callback  
  - Transaction Status Lookup  
  - Refund / Void (v6)  
  - Update Token  
  - Customer Checkout Redirect (Hosted Page)  
  - Email Payment Link  
  - Verify xPay  
  - mVISA QR Code  
- Transaction Payment Options  
- Super Wallet  
- Merchant Operations  
- xPay Payments  
  - Overview  
  - Execute xPay  
  - Check Balance  
- Reference & Codes  
  - Gateway Response Codes  
  - Verify Token Response Codes  
  - Missing Company Token  
- Plugins  
- DPO Pay API (v6 & v7) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Endpoint

HTTP: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

POST `https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Headers: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Request

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Field | Required | Description  
----- | -------- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token issued by DPO  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `verifyXpay`  
`XpayId` | Yes | xPay allocation ID to query  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Example Request (XML)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>verifyXpay</Request>
  <XpayId>67834</XpayId>
</API3G>
```


Response

You’ll receive a high-level `Result` and allocation details (sender/receiver, currency, amount, etc.). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Example Success Response (XML)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>Success</Result>
  <Status>Pending</Status>
  <Sender>Air Excel</Sender>
  <Receiver>Direct Pay Limited</Receiver>
  <Currency>USD</Currency>
  <Amount>0.40</Amount>
  <Description>Payment for flight</Description>
  <ServiceType>Safari Holiday</ServiceType>
</API3G>
```


(A “Test in Postman” link is also provided on the page.) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Fields

Field | Description  
----- | -----------  
`Result` | Result of the verify request (e.g., `Success`)  
`Status` | Allocation status (e.g., `Pending`, `Completed`, `Cancelled`)  
`Sender` | Merchant name that initiated the xPay  
`Receiver` | Merchant name that received the xPay  
`Currency` | Currency of the allocation  
`Amount` | Allocation amount  
`Description` | Allocation description / memo  
`ServiceType` | Service type label for the allocation  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

If your transaction responses elsewhere include xPay allocation references, you may also encounter `AllocationID` / `AllocationCode` in other APIs. Use `verifyXpay` to check the live status by `XpayId`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Typical Flow

1. Merchant (you) calls `verifyXpay` with `XpayId` to DPO API.  
2. DPO API returns `Result` plus allocation details (`Status`, `Sender`, `Receiver`, `Amount`, etc.).  
3. Merchant reconciles or displays status internally. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Best Practices

- Store and index `XpayId` in your back office so you can query status later.  
- Treat `Status` as the source of truth for allocation progress (`Pending` → `Completed`).  
- Log responses for audit trails (date, `XpayId`, `Status`, `Amount`, `Currency`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Troubleshooting

- If you receive a non-success `Result`, verify:  
  - `CompanyToken` validity  
  - That the `XpayId` exists and belongs to your hierarchy  
- For XML errors (e.g., `804`), confirm tag names and encoding.  
- If the allocation is tied to a wider transaction, cross-check the parent transaction via Transaction Status Lookup. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Page metadata

Updated: about 2 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-xpay)

Here’s the “mVISA QR Code” page content, cleaned for a `.txt` document. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

***

mVISA QR Code

Generate an mVISA-compatible QR payload string for a payment. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Create mVISA QR Code

You can create either a dynamic QR (tied to a specific `TransactionToken`) or a static QR (reusable) by setting `StaticQR`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

The API returns a payload string in `ResultExplanation`. Render that string as a QR image in your app/site using any standard QR library. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Endpoint

POST  
`https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Headers:

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Request

Fields: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Field | Required | Description  
----- | -------- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `createMvisaQRcode`  
`TransactionToken` | Yes | Use for dynamic QR tied to a specific transaction  
`StaticQR` | No | `1` to generate a static QR (default `0` = dynamic)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Dynamic vs Static: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

- Dynamic (recommended): include `TransactionToken`; the QR encodes a specific order and amount.  
- Static: set `StaticQR` = `1`; generates a merchant QR not tied to one token. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Example – Dynamic QR

XML structure: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Request>createMvisaQRcode</Request>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <TransactionToken>1639BBCE-0676-47BF-B0E1-ABC35402E25D</TransactionToken>
</API3G>
```



Example – Static QR

XML structure: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Request>createMvisaQRcode</Request>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <StaticQR>1</StaticQR>
</API3G>
```



Response

Success (Result `001`): [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>001</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>
    007834004328790355736269932231701153034045413981.0000000005802KE5925Direct Pay Online Test Ac6007Nairobi62060502186304212|4039 8410 0000 0061|Direct Pay Online Test Ac
  </ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

- `Result` = `001` → success  
- `ResultExplanation` → the QR payload string (EMV-style). Feed this text into a QR generator. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Error (Result `999`): [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>999</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Error</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

A “Test in Postman” link is available on the page. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

How to Render the QR

Use any standard QR library (frontend or backend). Pass the payload string from `ResultExplanation` to the generator. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Example (JavaScript, pseudo): [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

```javascript
// payload = value of ResultExplanation
QRCode.toCanvas(canvasElement, payload);
// or toDataURL / toString
```

Example (PHP, pseudo): [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

```php
// Using a QR lib like endroid/qr-code
$qrcode = QrCode::create($payload)->setSize(300);
```

Tip: For receipts/PDFs, generate a PNG from the payload and embed it. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Best Practices

- Prefer dynamic QR for one-time invoices and exact amounts (use `TransactionToken`).  
- Use static QR for countertop/printed codes where the amount is entered by the customer.  
- Log `Result`, a hash of `ResultExplanation`, `TransactionToken` (if any), and timestamp.  
- If you see `999 Error`, verify tag names/encoding and ensure your merchant is enabled for mVISA. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Typical Flow (Dynamic QR)

1. Merchant server calls `createToken` → receives `TransToken`.  
2. Merchant server calls `createMvisaQRcode` with `TransactionToken`.  
3. DPO returns `Result=001` with QR payload string.  
4. Merchant renders QR; customer scans & pays.  
5. DPO sends BackURL callback with result.  
6. Merchant may optionally call `verifyToken` for confirmation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Page metadata

Updated: about 2 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/mvisa-qr-code)

Overview – Transaction Payment Options

The **Transaction Payment Options** section provides all API operations required to fetch available payment methods and initiate charges using credit card, bank transfer, or mobile channels. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-payment-options-overview)

Use this section when you need to: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-payment-options-overview)

- Retrieve real-time payment method availability  
- Generate charges after a payment token has been created  
- Support multiple payment channels in your checkout flow  
- Implement fallback methods if a customer cannot complete the default payment option [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction-payment-options-overview)

Here’s the “Get Mobile Payment Options” page content, cleaned for a `.txt` document. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

***

Get Mobile Payment Options

Use `GetMobilePaymentOptions` to fetch the **available mobile money methods** for a specific transaction token (e.g., M-Pesa, Airtel, Vodacom). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

The response includes **country**, **name**, **logo**, **dial/USSD prefix**, **amount/currency**, and **step-by-step instructions** you can show to the customer. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

> This reads the merchant + token config and returns only the options that apply to that transaction. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

> Mobile money integrations are subject to country-specific requirements defined by Mobile Network Operators (MNOs), including supported networks, transaction limits, and approval flows. See the **MNO Advisory** for detailed guidance before enabling mobile payment options. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

***

Endpoint [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

***

Request [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

Field | Required | Description  
----- | -------- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `GetMobilePaymentOptions`  
`TransactionToken` | Yes | Token returned by `createToken`  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>GetMobilePaymentOptions</Request>
  <TransactionToken>72983CAC-5DB1-4C7F-BD88-352066B71592</TransactionToken>
</API3G>
```

***

Response [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

Returns one or more `<mobileoption>` items in the XML body. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <mobileoptions>
    <mobileoption>
      <country>kenya</country>
      <countryCode>KE</countryCode>
      <paymentname>airtel</paymentname>
      <logo>https://s3-eu-west-1.amazonaws.com/directpaystorage/airtel.png</logo>
      <celluarprefix>254</celluarprefix>
      <amount>120</amount>
      <currency>KES</currency>
      <instructions>
        1.Go to Airtel Money SIM toolkit;
        2.Select Airtel Money;
        3.Select 'Make payments';
        4.Select 'Pay bill';
        5.Select 'Other';
        6.Business name: 369369;
        7.Enter amount: 200;
        8.Enter Airtel Money PIN;
        9.Reference: 676CC8;
        10.OK to send.
      </instructions>
    </mobileoption>
    <mobileoption>
      <country>tanzania</country>
      <countryCode>TZ</countryCode>
      <paymentname>vodacom</paymentname>
      <logo>https://s3-eu-west-1.amazonaws.com/directpaystorage/vodacom.png</logo>
      <celluarprefix>255</celluarprefix>
      <amount>70</amount>
      <currency>TZS</currency>
      <instructions>
        1.Dial *150*00#;
        2.Select Pay by M-Pesa;
        3.Enter business number;
        4.Business: 644644;
        5.Reference: 676CC8;
        6.Amount: 4456.92;
        7.Enter PIN;
        8.Confirm (1) to proceed.
      </instructions>
    </mobileoption>
  </mobileoptions>
</API3G>
```

A “Test in Postman” link is also provided on the page. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

***

Field Reference (per `mobileoption`) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

Field | Description  
----- | -----------  
`country` / `countryCode` | Human name & ISO-2 code (e.g., `kenya` / `KE`)  
`paymentname` | Provider name (e.g., `airtel`, `vodacom`)  
`logo` | HTTPS URL to a provider logo you can display  
`celluarprefix` | Country calling code (e.g., `254`, `255`)  
`amount`, `currency` | Amount & ISO currency for this option  
`instructions` | Steps the customer follows to complete payment  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

> Note: Steps often include **business number** and **reference** values tied to the token (e.g., `CompanyRef` or a short code). Display them exactly as returned. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

***

Usage Notes & Best Practices [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

- Call after `createToken` and **before** you show mobile money choices to the customer.  
- Render each option with **logo + name + country**, and show a **“How to pay”** section using `instructions`.  
- Preserve line breaks/numbering in `instructions` (they are customer-facing).  
- If you support multiple regions, filter or sort options by `countryCode`.  
- Cache options **per token** briefly (they may depend on token amount/currency). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

***

Typical Flow [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

1. Merchant server calls `createToken` → receives `TransToken`.  
2. Merchant server calls `GetMobilePaymentOptions` with `TransactionToken`.  
3. DPO API returns list of mobile options & instructions.  
4. Merchant displays options; customer follows steps on their phone.  
5. DPO sends BackURL callback with payment result.  
6. (Optional) Merchant calls `verifyToken` for reconciliation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

***

Troubleshooting [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

- **Empty list**: Option not enabled for your merchant, or currency/amount not supported for that method.  
- **XML errors (`804`)**: Check exact tag names and encoding; ensure `Request` is `GetMobilePaymentOptions`.  
- **Logos not loading**: Ensure your front end allows HTTPS images from the S3 domain. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-mobile-payment-options)

***

Charge Token Auth

Use `chargeTokenAuth` to **capture/charge a transaction that has already been authorized** (e.g., the customer completed an auth on the hosted page or via a prior auth call). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

Think: **Auth → Capture**. If the transaction was never authorized, this call won’t proceed. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

***

Endpoint

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

***

Request

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

Field | Required | Description  
----- | -------- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `chargeTokenAuth`  
`TransactionToken` | Yes | Token returned by `createToken` (already **authorized**)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>chargeTokenAuth</Request>
  <TransactionToken>72983CAC-5DB1-4C7F-BD88-352066B71592</TransactionToken>
</API3G>
```



***

Response

Success (Queued for Capture) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transaction queued for charge</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

The charge is queued for DPO’s automated procedures. Final outcome will arrive via **BackURL (webhook)**; you can also call `verifyToken` for status. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

A “Test in Postman” link is provided on the page. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

***

Error Codes (common) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

Code | Explanation  
---- | -----------  
`000` | Transaction queued for charge  
`800` | Transaction **not authorized** yet (customer must authorize first, or use `chargeTokenCreditCard`)  
`801` | Missing `CompanyToken`  
`802` | `CompanyToken` does not exist  
`803` | Invalid/missing `Request` name  
`804` | Error in XML  
`902` | Data mismatch in one of the fields (see explanation text)  
`903` | Transaction **not found**  
`905` | Transaction **already charged**  
`950` | Missing mandatory field(s)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

***

When to Use

Use `chargeTokenAuth` when: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

- You operate an **Auth/Capture** flow (e.g., ship later, hotel pre-auth, car rental).  
- Customer has **already authorized** funds.  
- You now want to **capture** (charge) the funds. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

Do **not** use if: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

- The transaction was never authorized → first obtain authorization on the hosted page or via the appropriate auth flow.  
- You need to both authorize and capture in one go → use the standard hosted checkout sale flow (or `chargeTokenCreditCard` if applicable). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

***

Typical Flow (Auth/Capture)

1. Merchant calls `createToken`.  
2. Customer completes authorization on the hosted page (AUTH ONLY).  
3. DPO sends BackURL callback with authorized result.  
4. Merchant calls `chargeTokenAuth` to capture the auth.  
5. DPO returns `Result=000` (queued for charge).  
6. DPO sends BackURL callback with final capture result.  
7. (Optional) Merchant calls `verifyToken` for reconciliation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

***

Best Practices

- **Verify state first**: if you’re unsure it’s authorized, call **Transaction Status Lookup** (`verifyToken`). Authorized may appear as `001` in your verify-token codes table. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)
- Treat **BackURL** as the final truth; `chargeTokenAuth` only returns “queued”. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)
- Ensure idempotency: avoid duplicate captures by logging `(TransactionToken, action=capture)` and blocking repeats after success/queue. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)
- If you receive `800 Not authorized`:  
  - Ensure the original flow was **auth-only**, or  
  - Use the hosted page to complete auth, or  
  - Consider `chargeTokenCreditCard` if your flow supports it (direct charge with card details). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

***

Troubleshooting

- `905 Already charged`: capture already done; reconcile with `verifyToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)
- `903 Not found`: ensure `TransactionToken` is correct and not expired (PTL not elapsed before auth). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)
- `804 Error in XML`: check tag names and encoding exactly. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)
- No final confirmation: wait for BackURL or actively call `verifyToken` until you reach a terminal status. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

***

Updated: 4 months ago [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-auth)

***

Charge Token — Bank Transfer

Use `chargeTokenBankTransfer` to mark a token as **Pending Bank Transfer** and obtain the **converted amount & currency** for the selected bank. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

You must supply a **`BankCode`** previously obtained via **GetBankTransferOptions**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

After the customer pays at the bank, the transaction’s final status will update. Confirm via **BackURL webhook** and/or **verifyToken**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Endpoint

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Request

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Field | Required | Description  
----- | -------- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `chargeTokenBankTransfer`  
`TransactionToken` | Yes | Token returned by `createToken`  
`BankCode` | Yes | Bank identifier from **GetBankTransferOptions**  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Example Request (XML)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>chargeTokenBankTransfer</Request>
  <TransactionToken>72983CAC-5DB1-4C7F-BD88-352066B71592</TransactionToken>
  <BankCode>DTB</BankCode>
</API3G>
```


Response

Success [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transaction pending for bank transfer DTB</ResultExplanation>
  <ConvertedAmount>1.01</ConvertedAmount>
  <ConvertedCurrency>USD</ConvertedCurrency>
</API3G>
```

Error examples [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

```xml
<API3G>
  <Result>804</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Error in XML</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>

<API3G>
  <Result>950</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Request missing transaction level mandatory fields: BankCode</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>

<API3G>
  <Result>999</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Custom error message</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

Field reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Field | Meaning  
----- | -------  
`Result` | `000` = accepted / pending bank transfer  
`ResultExplanation` | Human-readable status (bank included)  
`ConvertedAmount` | Amount after conversion for the selected bank  
`ConvertedCurrency` | Currency used for the bank transfer  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

(A “Test in Postman” link is available on the page.) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Flow (Bank Transfer)

1. Merchant calls `createToken` → gets `TransactionToken`.  
2. Merchant calls **GetBankTransferOptions** → gets list of banks & `BankCode`s.  
3. Merchant calls `chargeTokenBankTransfer` with `TransactionToken + BankCode`.  
4. API returns `Result=000` plus `ConvertedAmount` / `ConvertedCurrency` (status = pending).  
5. Merchant shows bank details/instructions to the customer.  
6. Customer pays at the bank.  
7. DPO sends BackURL callback with updated status.  
8. (Optional) Merchant calls `verifyToken` for reconciliation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Usage Notes & Best Practices

- **Prerequisite:** call **GetBankTransferOptions** to obtain a valid `BankCode` for the token’s amount/currency.  
- Display the **ConvertedAmount/Currency** and bank instructions to the customer.  
- Treat **BackURL** as the source of truth for completion; use **verifyToken** if webhook is missed.  
- Log: `TransactionToken`, `BankCode`, `ConvertedAmount`, `ConvertedCurrency`, `Result`, `ResultExplanation`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Troubleshooting

- Wrong request name → ensure `Request` is `chargeTokenBankTransfer` (not `chargeTokenAuth`).  
- `950` missing fields → include `BankCode` exactly as returned by GetBankTransferOptions.  
- `804` XML error → verify tag names/encoding and that you included `TransactionToken`.  
- No final success → payment happens off-gateway; wait for webhook or poll `verifyToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Page metadata

Updated: 4 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Bottom navigation

Previous: Charge Token Auth  
Next: Charge Token — Credit Card [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-bank-transfer)

Here’s the “Charge Token — Credit Card” page content, cleaned for a `.txt` document. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

***

Charge Token — Credit Card
==========================

Use `chargeTokenCreditCard` to **charge a token directly with card details** (auth + capture in one call, unless your account is configured otherwise). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

> PCI Note: This operation requires you to **collect and transmit PAN/CVV** server-side. Do **not** use from browsers or mobile apps. Prefer the **Hosted Checkout** flow where possible. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)
