DPO PAY API (V7)  
- DPO Pay API Collection (v7) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Field | Required | Description  
----- | -------- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `chargeTokenCreditCard`  
`TransactionToken` | Yes | Token returned by `createToken`  
`CreditCardNumber` | Yes | PAN – no spaces  
`CreditCardExpiry` | Yes | `MMYY` (e.g. `1227`)  
`CreditCardCVV` | Yes | 3–4 digits  
`CardHolderName` | Yes | Name on card  
`ChargeType` | Optional | If supported (e.g. `Auth`, `Sale`) – tenant-specific  
`ThreeD` | Optional | 3-D Secure data object if doing 3DS off-gateway  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

If your tenant enforces 3-D Secure, provide `ThreeD` fields (see example); otherwise omit. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Example — Basic Card Charge (XML)
---------------------------------

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>chargeTokenCreditCard</Request>
  <TransactionToken>72983CAC-5DB1-4C7F-BD88-352066B71592</TransactionToken>
  <CreditCardNumber>4111111111111111</CreditCardNumber>
  <CreditCardExpiry>1227</CreditCardExpiry>
  <CreditCardCVV>123</CreditCardCVV>
  <CardHolderName>Alex Nkosi</CardHolderName>
</API3G>
```


Example — With 3-D Secure Data (XML)
------------------------------------

Field names vary by setup; the pattern below is common (confirm with DPO for your tenant). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>chargeTokenCreditCard</Request>
  <TransactionToken>72983CAC-5DB1-4C7F-BD88-352066B71592</TransactionToken>
  <CreditCardNumber>4111111111111111</CreditCardNumber>
  <CreditCardExpiry>1227</CreditCardExpiry>
  <CreditCardCVV>123</CreditCardCVV>
  <CardHolderName>Alex Nkosi</CardHolderName>
  <ThreeD>
    <eci>05</eci>
    <cavv>AAABBIc…base64…</cavv>
    <xid>MmY5…base64…</xid>
    <version>2.1.0</version>
  </ThreeD>
</API3G>
```


Response
--------

Success [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transaction charged</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

Errors (examples) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

```xml
<API3G>
  <Result>200</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transaction already paid</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>

<API3G>
  <Result>804</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Error in XML</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>

<API3G>
  <Result>902</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Data mismatch in one of the fields: CreditCardExpiry</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>

<API3G>
  <Result>950</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Request missing mandatory fields: CreditCardNumber</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

A “Test in Postman” link is provided on the page. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Common codes [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Code | Meaning  
---- | -------  
`000` | Transaction charged (success)  
`200` | Transaction already paid  
`801` | Missing `CompanyToken`  
`802` | `CompanyToken` does not exist  
`803` | Invalid request name  
`804` | XML error  
`902` | Data mismatch (field-specific)  
`903` | Transaction not found  
`905` | Transaction already charged  
`950` | Missing mandatory field(s)  

For full semantics after the charge, see **Gateway Response Codes (v6)** and **Verify Token Response Codes (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Flow (Direct Card Charge)
-------------------------

1. Merchant Server → DPO API: `createToken` → receive `TransactionToken`.  
2. Merchant Server → DPO API: `chargeTokenCreditCard` (PAN + CVV + Expiry + Token).  
3. DPO API → Merchant Server: immediate result (`Result=000` or error).  
4. (Optional) Merchant Server → DPO API: `verifyToken` for reconciliation.  
5. DPO → Merchant Server: BackURL callback (if configured) with final status. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Security & Compliance
---------------------

- Server-side only: do **not** send PAN/CVV from browser/mobile unless fully PCI compliant.  
- Do **not** log `CreditCardNumber` or `CreditCardCVV`; at most log masked last 4 digits.  
- Prefer **Hosted Checkout** or tokenization flows to reduce PCI scope.  
- If using 3DS off-gateway, transmit `ECI`, `CAVV`, `XID`, `version` exactly as provided by your ACS/3DS server. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Implementation Tips
-------------------

- Validate `MMYY` format for `CreditCardExpiry` before sending.  
- If you see `200 Already paid` or `905 Already charged`, stop and reconcile (do not re-charge).  
- Implement idempotency on `(TransactionToken, action=cardCharge)` to avoid duplicate charges on retries.  
- For declines/uncertain states, rely on **Transaction Status Lookup** and your **BackURL** webhook. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-credit-card)

Charge Token — Mobile
=====================

Use `ChargeTokenMobile` to initiate a **mobile money** request (e.g., M-Pesa/Airtel/Vodacom). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

You pass the **MSISDN (phone number)**, the **mobile network operator (MNO)**, and the **MNO’s country**. DPO returns actionable **customer instructions** and (sometimes) a **redirect URL requirement**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

> After the customer pays, the final status is delivered via **BackURL** and visible via **verifyToken**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/`

Headers [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml`

***

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

Field | Req | Description  
----- | --- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `ChargeTokenMobile`  
`TransactionToken` | Yes | Token from `createToken`  
`PhoneNumber` | Yes | MSISDN to charge (numeric, country rules apply)  
`MNO` | Yes | Mobile operator key (e.g., `mpesa`, `airtel`, `vodacom`)  
`MNOcountry` | Yes | Operator country name (e.g., `kenya`, `tanzania`)  

> Tip: If you’re unsure of valid `MNO` values for your tenant, first fetch options with **GetMobilePaymentOptions** and map the provider names to the accepted keys. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>ChargeTokenMobile</Request>
  <TransactionToken>9EF83250-B6A2-4FDD-A290-C4CE7EA6D447</TransactionToken>
  <PhoneNumber>254712345678</PhoneNumber>
  <MNO>mpesa</MNO>
  <MNOcountry>kenya</MNOcountry>
</API3G>
```

***

Response
--------

Success (invoice/push created) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <StatusCode>130</StatusCode>
  <ResultExplanation>New invoice</ResultExplanation>
  <instructions>
    Dear Customer,
    Shortly you will receive an M-PESA prompt on your phone requesting you to enter your M-PESA PIN to complete your payment.
    <br/>
    You can also pay using Lipa na MPESA:
    <br/>
    1. Go to the M-PESA menu
    <br/>
    2. Select Lipa na M-PESA
    <br/>
    3. Select Paybill
    <br/>
    4. Business number: 927633
    <br/>
    5. Account number: 2257FB0D1
    <br/>
    6. Amount: 1
    <br/>
    7. Enter PIN and confirm
  </instructions>
  <RedirectOption>0</RedirectOption>
</API3G>
```

A “Test in Postman” link is available on the page. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

Field | Meaning  
----- | -------  
`StatusCode` | Mobile request status (e.g., `130` = **New invoice**; some tenants show `0130`)  
`ResultExplanation` | Human-readable status  
`instructions` | Steps for the customer (HTML with `<br/>` for line breaks)  
`RedirectOption` | `1` = you must redirect customer to an MNO URL; `0` = no redirect required  

> When `RedirectOption=1`, DPO will typically include or return a URL you must open to complete the customer flow. Use exactly what DPO provides for your tenant. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

***

Error Codes (examples)
----------------------

Code | Meaning / Action  
---- | ----------------  
`801` | Missing `CompanyToken`  
`802` | `CompanyToken` invalid  
`803` | Bad or missing `Request` name  
`804` | XML error — check tags/encoding  
`950` | Missing mandatory fields  
`951` | Data mismatch – `TransactionToken`  
`952` | Missing `MNO`  
`953` | Missing `MNOcountry`  
`954` | Missing `PhoneNumber`  
`955` | **Invalid phone number** (format/range)  
`956` | **Terminal not found** (operator/country not enabled)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

***

Recommended Flow
----------------

1. Merchant → DPO: `createToken` → `TransactionToken`.  
2. (Optional) Merchant → DPO: `GetMobilePaymentOptions` for guidance.  
3. Merchant → DPO: `ChargeTokenMobile` (Token, MSISDN, MNO, country).  
4. DPO → Merchant: `StatusCode` + `instructions` (+ `RedirectOption`).  
5. Merchant: Show instructions / open MNO URL if required.  
6. Customer: Receives STK push/USSD, completes payment on phone.  
7. DPO → Merchant: BackURL callback with final result.  
8. (Optional) Merchant → DPO: `verifyToken` for reconciliation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

***

UX & Validation Tips
--------------------

- Validate MSISDN before sending (length/prefix per country).  
- Pre-fill `MNO` using your **GetMobilePaymentOptions** list.  
- Render `instructions` exactly, preserving line breaks (customer-facing).  
- If `RedirectOption=1`, immediately open the provided URL (new tab or in-app webview).  
- For pending flows, show “Waiting for prompt…” with cancel/retry options. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

***

Troubleshooting
---------------

Symptom | Likely Cause | Fix  
------- | ------------ | ---  
`955 Invalid phone number` | Wrong length/format | Normalize MSISDN (e.g., `2547…` for KE), remove spaces  
`956 Terminal not found` | MNO/country not enabled | Confirm enablement with DPO; align `MNO` key & casing  
No prompt on phone | Network delays or wrong operator | Let user retry; verify MSISDN & coverage  
Status stuck “pending” | Awaiting customer action | Wait for BackURL; poll `verifyToken`  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/charge-token-mobile)

***

Get Bank Transfer Options
=========================

Use `GetBankTransferOptions` to fetch **available bank transfer rails + instructions** for a specific transaction token.

You’ll receive a list of banks (each with a `bankCode`) and multilingual instructions you can render to customers.

> After the customer pays via bank transfer, confirm completion via **BackURL webhook** and/or **verifyToken**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/`

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

Request
-------

### Required Fields

Field | Required | Description  
----- | -------- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `GetBankTransferOptions`  
`TransactionToken` | Yes | Token returned by `createToken`  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

### Example Request (XML)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>GetBankTransferOptions</Request>
  <TransactionToken>9EF83250-B6A2-4FDD-A290-C4CE7EA6D447</TransactionToken>
</API3G>
``` 

Response
--------

On success (`Result=000`), the API returns a list with one or more entries. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

### Example Success Response (XML)

```xml
          Nome della Banca : Diamond Trust Bank;
          Filiale :T-Mall;
          Indirizzo della Banca : Langata Road/T - Mall, Nairobi, Kenya;
          Numero del Conto :0002725018;
          CODICE SWIFT : DTKEKENA;
          Aggiungi il seguente testo nella tua transazione (campo ulteriori informazioni) R73877558 ;
        </bankInstructionsIT>
        <bankInstructionsFR>
          Veuillez utiliser les détails ci-dessous pour votre virement bancaire;
          Nom du compte : 3G Direct Pay Limited;
          Nom de la banque : Diamond Trust Bank;
          Agence :T-Mall;
          Adresse de la banque : Langata Road/T - Mall, Nairobi, Kenya;
          Numéro de compte :0002725018;
          CODE SWIFT : DTKEKENA;
          Veuillez ajouter le texte suivant dans votre transaction (champ des informations supplémentaires) R73877558 ;
        </bankInstructionsFR>
        <bankInstructionsSW>
          Tafadhali tumia maelezo yaliyo chini kwa ajili ya uhamishaji wa benki;
          Jina la Akaunti : 3G Direct Pay Limited;
          Jina la Benki : Diamond Trust Bank;
          Tawi :T-Mall;
          Anwani ya Benki : Langata Road/T - Mall, Nairobi, Kenya;
          Namba ya Akaunti :0002725018;
          SWIFT CODE : DTKEKENA;
          Tafadhali ongeza maandishi yafuatayo katika mapatano (eneo la maelezo zaidi) R73877558 ;
        </bankInstructionsSW>
      </instructions>
    </option>

  </bankOptions>
</API3G>
```

> Some source samples show mis-encoded characters for accents; in your system, keep the verbatim text from the API, or normalize accents as needed for display. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

Field Reference
---------------

### Top-Level

Field | Description  
----- | -----------  
`Result` | `000` = Success; non-000 = error  
`ResultExplanation` | Human-readable status  
`bankOptions/option` | Repeated entries, one per available bank  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

### Each `option`

Field | Description  
----- | -----------  
`bankName` | Display name (often includes region/currency)  
`bankCode` | Code to pass to **chargeTokenBankTransfer**  
`instructions/*` | Multilingual blocks (`bankInstructionsEN`, `bankInstructionsIT`, `bankInstructionsFR`, `bankInstructionsSW`)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

Next Step: Mark Transaction as Pending (Bank Transfer)
------------------------------------------------------

After the shopper selects a bank, call **`chargeTokenBankTransfer`** with the chosen `bankCode`. That returns a **converted amount/currency** and sets status to **“Pending bank transfer”** until the funds arrive. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>chargeTokenBankTransfer</Request>
  <TransactionToken>9EF83250-B6A2-4FDD-A290-C4CE7EA6D447</TransactionToken>
  <BankCode>DTB</BankCode>
</API3G>
```

Then confirm completion via **BackURL** (webhook) or **verifyToken**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

A “Test in Postman” link is provided on the page. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

UI / UX Tips
------------

- Show each option as a **card**: `bankName`, language selector, and a **Copy All** button for the instructions.  
- If you know the shopper’s locale, default to that instruction block (EN, FR, SW, IT).  
- Keep the reference code (like `R73877558`) clearly visible.  
- Provide a “Mark as paid / I’ve completed the transfer” button explaining that your system will wait for DPO confirmation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

Troubleshooting
---------------

Symptom | Likely Cause | Action  
------- | ------------ | ------  
`Result != 000` | Missing/invalid fields | Ensure `Request=GetBankTransferOptions` and a valid `TransactionToken`  
Empty `bankOptions` | No bank rails for amount/currency/merchant | Adjust currency/amount or contact DPO  
XML `804` | Tag/encoding issue | Check capitalization and UTF-8 encoding  
Customer paid but no confirmation | Bank transfer not yet reconciled | Wait for **BackURL** or poll **verifyToken**  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

Typical Flow
------------

1. Merchant → DPO: `createToken` → `TransactionToken`.  
2. Merchant → DPO: `GetBankTransferOptions (TransactionToken)`.  
3. DPO → Merchant: `bankOptions` (list of banks + instructions).  
4. Merchant: Show bank cards + localized instructions.  
5. Customer: Performs bank transfer at their bank.  
6. Merchant → DPO: `chargeTokenBankTransfer (TransactionToken + bankCode)`.  
7. DPO → Merchant: `Result=000` (pending) + converted amount/currency.  
8. DPO → Merchant: BackURL callback when funds confirmed.  
9. (Optional) Merchant → DPO: `verifyToken` for reconciliation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-bank-transfer-options)

***

Company Mobile Payment Options
==============================

Use `CompanyMobilePaymentOptions` to fetch the **full set of mobile money rails** enabled on your merchant account (company‑wide).

This is useful for **configuration screens**, pre‑validating supported **MNO + country** pairs, or building a selector that later drives `ChargeTokenMobile`.

> For token‑specific options (amount/currency dependent), use **GetMobilePaymentOptions**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/`

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

Request
-------

### Required Fields

Field | Req | Description  
----- | --- | -----------  
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token  
`Request` | Yes | Must be `CompanyMobilePaymentOptions`  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

### Example Request (XML)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>CompanyMobilePaymentOptions</Request>
</API3G>
```


Response
--------

On success, returns a list of terminals/mobile options. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

### Example Success Response (XML)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <terminalmobile>
    <terminalredirecturi>0</terminalredirecturi>
    <terminaltype>Mobile</terminaltype>
    <terminalmno>SafaricomSTKv2</terminalmno>
    <terminalmnocountry>Kenya</terminalmnocountry>
  </terminalmobile>
  <terminalmobile>
    <terminalredirecturi>0</terminalredirecturi>
    <terminaltype>CL</terminaltype>
    <terminalmno>tigo</terminalmno>
    <terminalmnocountry>tanzania</terminalmnocountry>
  </terminalmobile>
</API3G>
```

(Example above is representative; your tenant may return more/fewer entries.)  
A “Test in Postman” link is provided on the page. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

Field Reference (per `terminalmobile`)
--------------------------------------

Field | Description  
----- | -----------  
`terminalredirecturi` | `1` = flow requires redirect to an operator URL; `0` = no redirect  
`terminaltype` | Terminal/type label (e.g., `Mobile`, `CL`)  
`terminalmno` | Mobile Network Operator key (use with `ChargeTokenMobile`)  
`terminalmnocountry` | Country name for this operator (e.g., `Kenya`, `tanzania`)  

> **Note:** `terminalmno` and `terminalmnocountry` must match what your tenant expects in `ChargeTokenMobile`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

When to Use Which
-----------------

- **CompanyMobilePaymentOptions** → show **all** mobile methods enabled for your merchant (good for **settings/config UI**).  
- **GetMobilePaymentOptions** → show **only** methods valid for a **specific token** (amount/currency‑dependent). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

Typical Flow
------------

**Admin / Config UI**

1. Call `CompanyMobilePaymentOptions`.  
2. Cache operator + country matrix.  

**Per Order / Token**

1. Call `GetMobilePaymentOptions`.  
2. Customer selects operator.  
3. Call `ChargeTokenMobile`.  
4. Receive BackURL / use `verifyToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

Usage Notes & Best Practices
----------------------------

- Build a **dropdown or card list** from `terminalmno` + `terminalmnocountry`.  
- If `terminalredirecturi=1`, be prepared to **open the operator URL** when charging.  
- Keep a **company‑wide mapping** and cross‑check it with token‑specific options for each transaction.  
- Normalize country values only in your **UI**; send values to the API **exactly as returned**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

Troubleshooting
---------------

Symptom | Likely Cause | Fix  
------- | ------------ | ---  
Empty list | No mobile rails enabled on merchant | Ask DPO to enable operators for your account  
XML `804` | Tag/encoding error | Ensure `Request=CompanyMobilePaymentOptions` and UTF‑8  
Operator rejected in `ChargeTokenMobile` | MNO/country mismatch vs tenant config | Use **exact** `terminalmno` + `terminalmnocountry` from this API  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/company-mobile-payment-options)

***

Overview – Super Wallet

The **Super Wallet** APIs enable you to securely store customer payment cards, generate reusable payment tokens, and perform one-click or recurring charges without requiring customers to re-enter their card details. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

This feature is designed for merchants who want to support: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

- Card-on-file payments  
- Tokenised transactions  
- Subscriptions and recurring billing  
- Faster repeat checkouts  
- Secure customer payment profiles [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

Super Wallet handles sensitive card data securely and returns tokens that can be safely stored and used for future charges. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

Super Wallet Workflow

Follow this step-by-step workflow to onboard customers into Super Wallet, save payment methods, generate subscription tokens, charge stored cards, retrieve transactions, and manage card lifecycle operations using the DPO Pay v6 API. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

Super Wallet Workflow – Open Recipe (interactive guide). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

What you can do with Super Wallet

Using the Super Wallet APIs, you can: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

- Create customer wallet accounts  
- Add and delete cards linked to a customer  
- Generate charge tokens for stored cards  
- Retrieve subscription tokens  
- Charge customers using tokens (including recurring charges)  
- Pull account details  
- Retrieve transaction history [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

Common use cases

- Saving a customer’s card for future purchases  
- Enabling one-click checkout  
- Implementing subscription billing  
- Charging customers on a schedule  
- Reducing PCI scope by using tokenised payments  
- Managing customer payment profiles programmatically [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

Typical flow

A common Super Wallet integration follows this pattern: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

1. **Create Account** – create a wallet profile for the customer  
2. **Add Card** – securely store the customer’s card  
3. **Generate Token** – obtain a charge or subscription token  
4. **Charge Token** – process payments using the stored token  
5. **Manage Wallet** – retrieve transactions or remove cards when required [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

High-level sequence (text version):

Start → Create account → Add card → Token needed →  
Create charge token / Create subscription token →  
Charge token / Charge token recurrent →  
Get transactions → Manage wallet → Pull account / Delete card → End [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

Security note

Card details are never reused directly after storage. All future transactions are performed using **tokens**, reducing exposure to sensitive data and improving compliance with security standards. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-overview)

Here’s the “Super Wallet – Get Transactions” page content, cleaned for a `.txt` document. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

***

Get Transactions (Super Wallet)

Use `SuperWalletGetTransactions` to retrieve all **transactions** paid for a specific **customer**, ordered by **payment date (descending)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

Common use: review a customer’s transaction history or reconcile wallet activity across multiple cards. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

***

Endpoint

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

Headers  
`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

***

Request

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

Field | Req | Description
----- | --- | -----------
`Request` | Yes | Must be `SuperWalletGetTransactions`
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Token provided by DPO to authorize API operations
`customerUnq` | Yes | Unique token identifying the customer
`customerToken` | No | Token for a specific credit card. If omitted, results include **all cards**
`numberOfRecords` | No | Max number of records to return (default: `100`)
`indexOfRecords` | No | Index of the first record to retrieve (default: `0`)

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>68B90B5E-25F6-4146-8AB1-C7A3A0C41A7F</CompanyToken>
  <Request>SuperWalletGetTransactions</Request>
  <customerUnq>9D3D99F7-3FEE-4792-961A-6EFFB5B642BA</customerUnq>
  <numberOfRecords>50</numberOfRecords>
  <indexOfRecords>25</indexOfRecords>
</API3G>
```


***

Response

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transactions found</ResultExplanation>
  <TotalTransactions>8</TotalTransactions>
  <transHistory>
    <trans>
      <transRef>49717D0F</transRef>
      <providerName>Direct Pay Online Payment</providerName>
      <transAmount>1.00</transAmount>
      <transCurrency>USD</transCurrency>
      <paymentDate>2018-07-20</paymentDate>
      <transCardType>MASC</transCardType>
      <transCardNum>(4679)</transCardNum>
    </trans>
    <trans>
      <transRef>49711B2E</transRef>
      <providerName>Direct Pay Online Payment</providerName>
      <transAmount>1.00</transAmount>
      <transCurrency>USD</transCurrency>
      <paymentDate>2018-07-20</paymentDate>
      <transCardType>MASC</transCardType>
      <transCardNum>(3215)</transCardNum>
    </trans>
  </transHistory>
</API3G>
```



Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

Field | Description
----- | -----------
`Result` | Response code returned by the server
`ResultExplanation` | Description of the result
`TotalTransactions` | Total number of transactions found (for this query)
`transHistory` | Array of transaction objects
`transRef` | Transaction reference
`providerName` | Payment provider name
`transAmount` | Transaction amount
`transCurrency` | Currency code (e.g., USD, KES)
`paymentDate` | Date of transaction
`transCardType` | Card type used (e.g., VISA, MASC)
`transCardNum` | Masked card number (last 4 digits)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

***

Typical Usage Flow

1. Merchant → DPO API: `SuperWalletGetTransactions` (CompanyToken, customerUnq, optional filters).  
2. DPO API → Merchant: result + `TotalTransactions` + `transHistory`.  
3. Merchant: display transactions ordered by payment date (descending).  
4. Optionally repeat call with `indexOfRecords` for pagination. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

***

Notes & Best Practices

- Use pagination (`numberOfRecords`, `indexOfRecords`) for large result sets.  
- If `customerToken` is **not** provided, all transactions for the customer’s Super Wallet are returned.  
- Transactions are listed **newest first**.  
- Always check `Result` and `ResultExplanation` before parsing data.  
- Store responses securely if used for financial reporting or reconciliation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

***

Common Result Codes

Code | Meaning | Action
---- | ------- | ------
`000` | Transactions found | Success
`801` | Missing `CompanyToken` | Provide valid token
`804` | XML error | Check formatting/encoding
`902` | Data mismatch | Verify `customerUnq` or `customerToken`
`999` | Internal error | Retry or contact support

 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

Updated: 5 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-transactions)

Here’s the “Recurring Payments (Tokenisation Guide)” page content, cleaned for a `.txt` document. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

***

Recurring Payments (Tokenisation Guide)
=======================================

Recurring payments in **DPO Pay v6** are enabled using **Super Wallet tokenisation**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

During the initial payment, the customer’s card is securely saved and associated with a **Subscription Token**. This token can then be used to charge the customer again without requiring them to re-enter their card details. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Recurring payments are commonly used for: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

- subscriptions  
- memberships  
- instalment billing  
- scheduled payments  

Recurring Payment Flow
======================

The recurring payment process consists of the following steps: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

1. **Create an initial transaction token**  
2. **Enable recurrence during the first payment**  
3. **Verify the payment**  
4. **Retrieve the customer’s subscription token**  
5. **Charge the saved payment method for future payments** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

High-level flow:

Create Token → Customer completes payment → Verify Token → Retrieve Subscription Token → Charge Token Recurrent [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Step 1 — Create the Initial Payment Token
=========================================

Start by creating a transaction using the **`createToken`** request. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

To enable recurring payments, include the following parameter inside the transaction request: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

- A flag in the XML set to `1` to indicate that the customer’s payment method should be stored for recurrence (tokenisation enabled). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

This tells the gateway to save the customer’s payment details for future recurring charges. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

After creating the token, redirect the customer to the hosted payment page to complete the transaction. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Step 2 — Verify the Initial Transaction
=======================================

Once the customer completes the payment, confirm the transaction using the **`verifyToken`** request. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

This step ensures the initial payment was successful before attempting to store or reuse the payment method. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Step 3 — Retrieve the Subscription Token
========================================

After the successful payment, retrieve the **`SubscriptionToken`** using the **`getSubscriptionToken`** request. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

This token identifies the saved payment method associated with the customer. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

The response typically includes: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

- **SubscriptionToken** – identifier for the saved payment method  
- **CustomerToken** – identifier for the customer  

These values are required for future recurring charges. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Step 4 — Charge the Saved Payment Method
========================================

To perform a recurring charge: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

1. Create a new transaction token using **`createToken`**.  
2. Use the **`chargeTokenRecurrent`** request with:  
   - `TransactionToken`  
   - `SubscriptionToken` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

This will charge the customer’s saved card without requiring further input from the customer. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Step 5 — Managing Stored Cards
==============================

If required, stored payment methods can be removed using the **`deleteCard`** request. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

This allows merchants to remove a saved card or subscription from the Super Wallet. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Try it as a guided flow
=======================

Follow a step-by-step implementation using the **Recurring Subscription (Tokenised Payments)** recipe. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

- Recurring Subscription (Tokenised Payments) – Open Recipe [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Related API Endpoints
=====================

The following Super Wallet endpoints are used for recurring payments: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Endpoint | Description  
-------- | -----------  
`createToken` | Create a transaction token  
`verifyToken` | Verify the initial transaction  
`getSubscriptionToken` | Retrieve stored payment token  
`chargeTokenRecurrent` | Charge a saved payment method  
`deleteCard` | Remove stored card  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Each endpoint is documented in the **Super Wallet API Reference**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Important Notes
===============

- The first transaction must include the recurrence flag set to `1` to enable tokenisation.  
- Recurring payments require a valid **SubscriptionToken**.  
- The initial transaction must be successfully verified before performing recurring charges. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Updated: 18 days ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Next: Add Card [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/recurring-payments-tokenisation-guide)

Add Card
========

Use `addCard` to **add a new credit card** to an existing Super Wallet account (customer).

If 3-D Secure (3DS) data is provided, the card can be verified during the add step.

> Common use: enroll a customer’s card for future payments and refunds (tokenised), optionally verifying via 3DS. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Navigation context (Super Wallet)
---------------------------------

Super Wallet section includes: Overview, Get Transactions, Recurring Payments (Tokenisation Guide), Add Card, Create Account, Customer Charge Token, Get Subscription Token, Pull Account, Charge Token Recurrent, Delete Card. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Field | Type | Req | Description
----- | ---- | --- | -----------
`Request` | string | Yes | Must be `addCard`
`CompanyToken` | string | Yes | Token provided by DPO to authorise API operations
`customerToken` | string | Yes | Customer token (from `createAccount`)
`CustomerCreditCard` | string | Yes | Credit card number (PAN)
`CustomerExpiry` | string | Yes | Card expiry. Format: `MMYY` (e.g. `1225`) – some integrations accept `MM/YY`, but `MMYY` is recommended for v6
`CustomerCvv` | string | Yes | Card CVV/CVC
`CustomerHolderName` | string | Yes | Cardholder name
`CustomerAllowSWrefunds` | integer | No | Verify card via current company account (default `0`)
`CustomerThreeD` | object | No | 3-D Secure verification payload

CustomerThreeD object [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Field | Type | Description
----- | ---- | -----------
`Enrolled` | string | Enrollment status from directory server
`Paresstatus` | string | PARes status (e.g. `Y`, `N`)
`Eci` | string | Electronic Commerce Indicator (e.g. `05`, `06`)
`Xid` | string | Transaction identifier
`Cavv` | string | CAVV/AVV value
`Signature` | string | 3DS signature/result
`Veres` | string | Verification result (e.g. `AUTHENTICATION_SUCCESSFUL`)
`Pares` | string | PARes content (base64/encoded)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Example Request (XML)
---------------------

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>68B90B5E-25F6-4146-8AB1-C7A3A0C41A7F</CompanyToken>
  <Request>addCard</Request>
  <customerToken>E6C04D7E-C267-4243-BD1C-49170F8A008B</customerToken>
  <CustomerCreditCard>4111111111111111</CustomerCreditCard>
  <CustomerExpiry>1225</CustomerExpiry>
  <CustomerCvv>123</CustomerCvv>
  <CustomerHolderName>Josh</CustomerHolderName>
  <CustomerAllowSWrefunds>1</CustomerAllowSWrefunds>
  <CustomerThreeD>
    <Enrolled>Y</Enrolled>
    <Paresstatus>Y</Paresstatus>
    <Eci>05</Eci>
    <Xid>DYYVcrwnujRMnHDy1wlP1Ggz8w0=</Xid>
    <Cavv>mHyn+7YFi1EUAREAAAAvNUe6Hv8=</Cavv>
    <Signature>_</Signature>
    <Veres>AUTHENTICATION_SUCCESSFUL</Veres>
    <Pares>eAHNV1mzokgW/is</Pares>
  </CustomerThreeD>
</API3G>
```

> Note: Sample values are illustrative. Provide only valid 3DS fields returned by your ACS/Directory Server. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Response
--------

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Card verified</ResultExplanation>
  <customerToken>9C6BB1D2-B2DE-46B3-8AD7-409168936DDA</customerToken>
  <subscriptionToken>977E056D-3AD2-4DC5-AE8A-3B8CFF00741A</subscriptionToken>
  <cardType>Visa</cardType>
  <cardLast4>2222</cardLast4>
</API3G>
```

Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Field | Type | Description
----- | ---- | -----------
`Result` | integer | Result code
`ResultExplanation` | string | Human-readable explanation
`customerToken` | string | Customer token (use for future wallet operations)
`subscriptionToken` | string | Tokenised card reference for payments/subscriptions
`cardType` | string | Card brand (e.g. `Visa`, `Mastercard`)
`cardLast4` | string | Last 4 digits of the card  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Result Codes (from spec)
------------------------

Code | Explanation
---- | -----------
`000` | Successful – Card verified
`999` | Dynamic error (based on XML sent)
`950` | Dynamic error (based on XML sent)

Common v6 codes you may also encounter: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Code | Meaning | Action
---- | ------- | ------
`801` | Missing `CompanyToken` | Provide a valid token
`803` | Bad/missing `Request` name | Ensure `addCard`
`804` | XML error | Check tag names/encoding
`902` | Data mismatch | Verify `customerToken` and 3DS fields

Typical Usage Flow
------------------

1. Merchant (server) calls `addCard` with PAN, Expiry, CVV, Holder, `customerToken`.  
2. Optional: include `CustomerThreeD` (ECI, CAVV, XID, etc.) when 3DS is available.  
3. DPO returns `Result` plus `subscriptionToken`, `cardType`, `cardLast4`.  
4. Merchant stores tokens (not PAN/CVV).  
5. Merchant uses `subscriptionToken` for future charges (e.g. `customerChargeToken`, `chargeTokenRecurrent`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Notes & Best Practices
----------------------

- PCI-DSS: Do **not** log or store `CustomerCreditCard` or `CustomerCvv`. Persist only `customerToken` and `subscriptionToken`.  
- Expiry format: Prefer `MMYY` (e.g. `1225`). If you used `MM/YY` previously, standardise to `MMYY` for v6 unless told otherwise.  
- 3DS: When available, pass `CustomerThreeD` to add a **verified** card on enrolment. Validate ECI/CAVV/XID for successful 3DS results.  
- Refunds via Super Wallet: Set `CustomerAllowSWrefunds=1` when you want the card verified via the current company account to allow SW refunds.  
- Idempotency: If you may retry, implement your own de-duplication key to avoid unintended duplicate card entries.  
- Security: Always use TLS, mask PAN in UIs, and restrict access to tokens. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Metadata & Navigation
---------------------

Updated: 5 months ago.

Next: Create Account [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-add-card)

Create Account
==============

Use `createAccount` to **create a new Super Wallet account** for a customer.

If card details are provided, the API attempts to verify the card by charging **0.15 USD** (a temporary authorization).

> Common use: onboard a customer into Super Wallet and tokenize their first payment card in one call. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

Field | Type | Req | Description
----- | ---- | --- | -----------
`Request` | string | Yes | Must be `createAccount`
`CompanyToken` | string | Yes | Token provided by DPO to authorize API operations
`CustomerEmail` | string | Yes | Customer email address
`CustomerFirstName` | string | Yes | Customer first name
`CustomerLastName` | string | Yes | Customer last name
`CustomerPhone` | string | Yes | Customer phone number
`CustomerDialCode` | string | Yes | Customer country ISO-2 code (e.g., `ZA`, `KE`, `NG`)
`CustomerPassword` | string | No | Minimum 6 characters; supports `!@#$%&()?`
`CustomerAddress` | string | No | Customer address
`CustomerCity` | string | No | Customer city
`CustomerCountry` | string | No | Country ISO-2 code (e.g., `KE`, `UG`)
`CustomerZip` | string | No | Postal/ZIP code
`CustomerNoCard` | integer | No | `1` = create account **without** card; `0` = create with card (default `0`)
`CustomerCreditCard` | string | Conditional | Required if `CustomerNoCard = 0`
`CustomerExpiry` | string | Conditional | Required if `CustomerNoCard = 0` – format `MMYY`
`CustomerCvv` | string | Conditional | Required if `CustomerNoCard = 0`
`CustomerHolderName` | string | Conditional | Required if `CustomerNoCard = 0`
`CustomerAllowSWrefunds` | string | No | Verify card via current company account (default `0`)
`CustomerThreeD` | object | No | 3-D Secure verification object (optional)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

CustomerThreeD object [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

Field | Type | Description
----- | ---- | -----------
`Enrolled` | string | Enrollment status
`Paresstatus` | string | PARes status (e.g., `Y`, `N`)
`Eci` | string | Electronic Commerce Indicator (e.g., `05`, `06`)
`Xid` | string | Transaction identifier
`Cavv` | string | CAVV/AVV value
`Signature` | string | 3DS signature result
`Veres` | string | Verification result
`Pares` | string | PARes content (base64/encoded)

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>8D3DA73D-9D7F-4E09-96D4-3D44E7A83EA3</CompanyToken>
  <Request>createAccount</Request>
  <CustomerEmail>test@directpay.online</CustomerEmail>
  <CustomerFirstName>Josh</CustomerFirstName>
  <CustomerLastName>Grinberg</CustomerLastName>
  <CustomerAddress>Rose Avenue 14</CustomerAddress>
  <CustomerCity>Nairobi</CustomerCity>
  <CustomerCountry>KE</CustomerCountry>
  <CustomerDialCode>KE</CustomerDialCode>
  <CustomerPhone>0553231231</CustomerPhone>
  <CustomerZip>762132</CustomerZip>
  <CustomerCreditCard>4111111111111111</CustomerCreditCard>
  <CustomerExpiry>1225</CustomerExpiry>
  <CustomerCvv>123</CustomerCvv>
  <CustomerHolderName>Josh Grinberg</CustomerHolderName>
  <CustomerAllowSWrefunds>1</CustomerAllowSWrefunds>
  <CustomerThreeD>
    <Enrolled>Y</Enrolled>
    <Paresstatus>Y</Paresstatus>
    <Eci>05</Eci>
    <Xid>DYYVcrwnujRMnHDy1wlP1Ggz8w0=</Xid>
    <Cavv>mHyn+7YFi1EUAREAAAAvNUe6Hv8=</Cavv>
    <Signature>_</Signature>
    <Veres>AUTHENTICATION_SUCCESSFUL</Veres>
    <Pares>eAHNV1mzokgW/is</Pares>
  </CustomerThreeD>
</API3G>
```

> If `CustomerNoCard=1`, omit all card-related fields. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

Response
--------

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Card verified</ResultExplanation>
  <customerToken>9C6BB1D2-B2DE-46B3-8AD7-409168936DDA</customerToken>
  <subscriptionToken>977E056D-3AD2-4DC5-AE8A-3B8CFF00741A</subscriptionToken>
  <cardType>Visa</cardType>
  <cardLast4>2222</cardLast4>
</API3G>
```

Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

Field | Type | Description
----- | ---- | -----------
`Result` | integer | Response code
`ResultExplanation` | string | Human-readable explanation
`customerToken` | string | Unique customer token (used for Super Wallet operations)
`subscriptionToken` | string | Tokenized card reference for future payments/subscriptions
`cardType` | string | Credit card brand
`cardLast4` | string | Last 4 digits of card number

Result Codes [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

Code | ResultExplanation | Meaning / Action
---- | ----------------- | ----------------
`000` | Card verified | Success – account and card created
`999` | Account created, card not verified | Retry or add card later
`803` | No or invalid request name | Ensure `Request=createAccount`
`888` | System error | Retry or contact support
`902` | Data mismatch | Verify request fields
`950` | Missing mandatory fields | Add missing tag(s)
`991` | Encrypted string empty | Encryption or formatting error

Typical Usage Flow [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

1. Merchant → DPO API: `createAccount` (customer + optional card details).  
2. DPO API → Merchant:  
   - `Result=000` → account + card verified, tokens returned.  
   - `Result=999` → account created, card not verified (retry or add card later with `addCard`).  
3. Merchant: stores `customerToken` and (if present) `subscriptionToken`.  

Notes & Best Practices [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

- Verification charge: card verification uses a **0.15 USD** authorization.  
- Without card: set `CustomerNoCard=1` to create an account without a card.  
- PCI compliance: never log or store full PAN or CVV; keep only tokens.  
- 3-D Secure: when present, `CustomerThreeD` allows pre-verification of cards during account creation.  
- Token usage: `customerToken` and `subscriptionToken` are required for Super Wallet operations like `addCard`, `customerChargeToken`, `SuperWalletGetTransactions`.  

Updated: 5 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-create-account)

***

Customer Charge Token
=====================

Use `customerChargeToken` to **charge a customer’s stored card** using their existing Super Wallet tokens. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

This request completes a payment by referencing both the **customerToken** and the **paymentToken** (subscription token). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

> Common use: perform payments for returning customers without collecting card details again. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

DPO PAY API (V7)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

Field | Type | Req | Description
----- | ---- | --- | -----------
`Request` | string | Yes | Must be `customerChargeToken`
`CompanyToken` | string | Yes | Token provided by DPO to authorize API operations
`TransactionToken` | string | Yes | Token of the transaction to be charged
`customerToken` | string | Yes | Customer’s Super Wallet token
`paymentToken` | string | Yes | Tokenized card reference (subscription token)
`paymentTokenCVV` | integer | No | Card CVV — if mandatory, the API will respond instructing you to resend with CVV

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>68B90B5E-25F6-4146-8AB1-C7A3A0C41A7F</CompanyToken>
  <Request>customerChargeToken</Request>
  <TransactionToken>3AB58C3C-796F-4FA9-A333-72E75250778E</TransactionToken>
  <customerToken>9C6BB1D2-B2DE-46B3-8AD7-409168936DDA</customerToken>
  <paymentToken>977E056D-3AD2-4DC5-AE8A-3B8CFF00741A</paymentToken>
  <paymentTokenCVV>111</paymentTokenCVV>
</API3G>
```

> If the response indicates that CVV is required, re-submit the same request including `paymentTokenCVV`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

Response
--------

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transaction successful</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

Field | Type | Description
----- | ---- | -----------
`Result` | integer | Response code returned by the API
`ResultExplanation` | string | Free-text explanation of the result

Result Codes
------------

Code | ResultExplanation | Meaning / Action
---- | ----------------- | ----------------
`000` | Transaction successful | Payment processed successfully
`888` | System error | Retry or contact support
`999` | Customer not found / Account verification required | Ensure customer account is created and verified
`902` | Data mismatch | Verify transaction and token fields
`950` | Missing mandatory fields | Check XML structure and required tags
`803` | No or invalid request name | Confirm `Request=customerChargeToken`
`991` | Encrypted string is empty | Check encryption and formatting  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

Typical Usage Flow
------------------

1. Create a Super Wallet account (`createAccount`) and store `customerToken`.  
2. Store a card and get `subscriptionToken` (used as `paymentToken`).  
3. Create a transaction token (`createToken`).  
4. Call `customerChargeToken` with `CompanyToken`, `TransactionToken`, `customerToken`, `paymentToken`, and optionally `paymentTokenCVV`.  
5. Check `Result` / `ResultExplanation`, then confirm via `verifyToken` or BackURL if needed. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

Notes & Best Practices
----------------------

- **Tokenized payments:** Use this endpoint for returning customers; the customer does not re-enter card details.  
- **CVV handling:** Some issuers require CVV for stored-card transactions — only send `paymentTokenCVV` when prompted, and never log it.  
- **Security:** Store only `customerToken` and `paymentToken` (subscription token); never store PAN/CVV.  
- **Idempotency:** Avoid duplicate charges by tracking `TransactionToken` at your application level and not retrying blindly.  
- **Response validation:** Always check both `Result` and `ResultExplanation` before updating payment status in your system.  
- **Error recovery:** Retry only for transient issues (e.g., `888`), not for data/verification errors. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

Updated: 5 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-customer-charge-token)

Previous: Create Account  
Next: Get Subscription Token

Here’s the “Get Subscription Token” page content, cleaned for a `.txt` document. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Get Subscription Token
======================

Use `getSubscriptionToken` to **retrieve a customer’s Super Wallet tokens** (both the subscription token and the customer token). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

This is useful when you need to re-establish a customer session or verify tokens for returning users. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

> Common use: recover a customer’s saved payment tokens using their **Email** or **Phone number**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Field | Type | Req | Description
----- | ---- | --- | -----------
`Request` | string | Yes | Must be `getSubscriptionToken`
`CompanyToken` | string | Yes | Token provided by DPO to authorize API operations
`SearchCriteria` | integer | Yes | How to identify the customer: `1` = by **Email**, `2` = by **Phone number**
`SearchCriteriaValue` | string | Yes | Email address or phone number (depending on `SearchCriteria`)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>68B90B5E-25F6-4146-8AB1-C7A3A0CAABB3</CompanyToken>
  <Request>getSubscriptionToken</Request>
  <SearchCriteria>1</SearchCriteria>
  <SearchCriteriaValue>test@directpay.online</SearchCriteriaValue>
</API3G>
```

> Tip: Use `SearchCriteria=1` (email) for most integrations. Use `2` (phone number) when the customer was registered primarily by mobile. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Response
--------

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Success</ResultExplanation>
  <SubscriptionToken>37CB51E6-EF18-4E27-A80E-8448B7B0342A</SubscriptionToken>
  <CustomerToken>C1E0F067-DFB9-4CA0-8CC2-FCC6018243B3</CustomerToken>
</API3G>
```

Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Field | Type | Description
----- | ---- | -----------
`Result` | integer | Response code
`ResultExplanation` | string | Description of the response
`SubscriptionToken` | string | The customer’s **subscription token** (payment token)
`CustomerToken` | string | The **customer’s unique Super Wallet token**  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Result Codes
------------

Code | ResultExplanation | Meaning / Action
---- | ----------------- | ----------------
`000` | Success | Tokens retrieved successfully
`803` | Invalid or missing `Request` name | Ensure `Request=getSubscriptionToken`
`888` | System error | Retry or contact support
`902` | Data mismatch | Verify `SearchCriteria` and `SearchCriteriaValue`
`950` | Missing mandatory fields | Check XML tags and required fields
`991` | Encrypted string empty | Invalid or corrupted request
`999` | Customer not found | Ensure customer exists or create via `createAccount`  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Typical Usage Flow
------------------

1. Merchant → DPO API: `getSubscriptionToken` (CompanyToken, SearchCriteria, SearchCriteriaValue).  
2. DPO API → Merchant: `Result=000` + `SubscriptionToken` + `CustomerToken`.  
3. Merchant: store or refresh local tokens for future `customerChargeToken` or `addCard` calls. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Notes & Best Practices
----------------------

- **Use cases:** retrieve existing customer tokens to enable auto-payments or re-link wallets.  
- **Search behaviour:**  
  - `SearchCriteria=1` → provide customer **email address**.  
  - `SearchCriteria=2` → provide customer **phone number** (including country code).  
- **Security:** tokens uniquely identify wallet accounts; handle and store them securely.  
- **Verification:** always confirm `Result=000` before using returned tokens.  
- **Fallback:** if you receive `999 Customer not found`, prompt the user to register via `createAccount`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Updated: 5 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-get-subscription-token)

Pull Account
============

Use `pullAccount` to **retrieve a registered customer’s saved payment tokens** and available payment options. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

This request returns all stored cards or other payment methods linked to a specific Super Wallet customer. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

> Common use: retrieve stored payment tokens (e.g., cards) to display as selectable options during checkout. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Field | Type | Req | Description
----- | ---- | --- | -----------
`Request` | string | Yes | Must be `pullAccount`
`CompanyToken` | string | Yes | Token provided by DPO to authorize API operations
`customerToken` | string | Yes | Token identifying the customer (from `createAccount`)  

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>68B90B5E-25F6-4146-8AB1-C7A3A0C41A7F</CompanyToken>
  <Request>pullAccount</Request>
  <customerToken>E6C04D7E-C267-4243-BD1C-49170F8A008B</customerToken>
</API3G>
```

> Tip: Use this endpoint to show customers their saved cards, digital wallets, or payment methods for quicker checkouts. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Response
--------

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Success</ResultExplanation>
  <customerToken>E6C04D7E-C267-4243-BD1C-49170F8A008B</customerToken>
  <paymentOptions>
    <paymentOption>
      <subscriptionToken>9C6BB1D2-B2DE-46B3-8AD7-409168936DDA</subscriptionToken>
      <paymentType>Mastercard</paymentType>
      <paymentLast4>0015</paymentLast4>
    </paymentOption>
  </paymentOptions>
</API3G>
```

Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Field | Type | Description
----- | ---- | -----------
`Result` | integer | Result code returned by the server
`ResultExplanation` | string | Human-readable explanation of the response
`customerToken` | string | Customer’s Super Wallet token
`paymentOptions` | array | Contains one or more `paymentOption` entries
`subscriptionToken` | string | Tokenized reference for the stored payment method
`paymentType` | string | Payment type or card brand (e.g., `Visa`, `Mastercard`, `Mobile`)
`paymentLast4` | string | Last 4 digits of the stored card or phone number  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Result Codes
------------

Code | ResultExplanation | Meaning / Action
---- | ----------------- | ----------------
`000` | Success | Tokens retrieved successfully
`803` | Invalid or missing `Request` name | Ensure `pullAccount`
`888` | System error | Retry or contact support
`902` | Data mismatch | Verify `customerToken`
`950` | Missing mandatory fields | Add missing tags
`991` | Encrypted string empty | Request formatting issue
`999` | Customer not found | Ensure account was created and verified  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Typical Usage Flow
------------------

1. Merchant → DPO API: `pullAccount` (CompanyToken, customerToken).  
2. DPO API → Merchant: `Result=000` + `paymentOptions` (each with `subscriptionToken`, `paymentType`, `paymentLast4`).  
3. Merchant: display available stored cards or wallets for customer selection.  
4. Merchant: use chosen `subscriptionToken` for future charges via `customerChargeToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Notes & Best Practices
----------------------

- Use case: display a customer’s saved cards or payment methods for faster checkout.  
- Token handling: store only `subscriptionToken` and `paymentType` — never full PAN or CVV.  
- Customer verification: ensure the `customerToken` is valid and active before calling this API.  
- Multiple payment options: customers may have several saved methods; always iterate over all entries.  
- Security: handle token data securely; these tokens act as authorization credentials for subsequent payments.  
- Error handling: always check both `Result` and `ResultExplanation` before displaying payment options. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Updated: 5 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-pull-account)

Charge Token Recurrent
======================

Use `chargeTokenRecurrent` to **process a recurring charge** for a customer who has previously subscribed and stored a payment token with your company. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

This request allows you to bill a customer automatically using their **subscription token**, without requiring them to re-enter card details. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

> Common use: automate subscription payments or recurring billing for verified Super Wallet customers. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

Request
-------

### Required Fields

Field | Type | Req | Description
----- | ---- | --- | -----------
`Request` | string | Yes | Must be `chargeTokenRecurrent`
`CompanyToken` | string | Yes | Token provided by DPO to authorize API operations
`TransactionToken` | string | Yes | Token of the transaction to be charged
`subscriptionToken` | string | Yes | Tokenized card reference of the subscribed customer  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

### Example Request (XML)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>68B90B5E-25F6-4146-8AB1-C7A3A0C41A7F</CompanyToken>
  <Request>chargeTokenRecurrent</Request>
  <TransactionToken>3AB58C3C-796F-4FA9-A333-72E75250778E</TransactionToken>
  <subscriptionToken>9C6BB1D2-B2DE-46B3-8AD7-409168936DDA</subscriptionToken>
</API3G>
```


> Use this API for recurring payments, such as subscriptions, memberships, or scheduled billing cycles. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

Response
--------

### Example Success Response (XML)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Transaction successful</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```


### Field Reference

Field | Type | Description
----- | ---- | -----------
`Result` | integer | Response code returned by the API
`ResultExplanation` | string | Text message describing the result  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

Result Codes
------------

Code | ResultExplanation | Meaning / Action
---- | ----------------- | ----------------
`000` | Transaction successful | Payment completed successfully
`803` | Invalid or missing `Request` name | Ensure `chargeTokenRecurrent`
`888` | System error | Retry or contact support
`902` | Data mismatch | Verify `TransactionToken` or `subscriptionToken`
`950` | Missing mandatory fields | Check XML payload for missing tags
`991` | Encrypted string empty | Check encryption or formatting
`999` | Customer not found or unverified | Ensure tokens are active and verified  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

Typical Usage Flow
------------------

1. Merchant → DPO API: `chargeTokenRecurrent` (CompanyToken, TransactionToken, subscriptionToken).  
2. DPO API → Merchant: `Result=000` + `ResultExplanation=Transaction successful`.  
3. Merchant: mark subscription renewal as paid and, if required, confirm via `verifyToken` / BackURL callback. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

Notes & Best Practices
----------------------

- **Purpose:** Designed for **recurring** or **scheduled** payments for previously subscribed customers. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)
- **Prerequisite:** The customer must have an active Super Wallet account with a valid `subscriptionToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)
- **Security:** Never expose or log tokens. Handle them with the same care as sensitive payment data. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)
- **Error handling:**  
  - `000` → success — mark the invoice/renewal as paid.  
  - `999` → customer unverified or not found — prompt re-verification or re-enrolment.  
  - `950` → missing field — fix XML and resend. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)
- **Retries:** Only retry on transient failures (e.g., `888` system error). Avoid duplicate billing attempts. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)
- **Automation:** Ideal for scheduled backend jobs, CRON tasks, or automated billing workflows. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent)

Updated: 5 months ago.
