Delete Card
===========

Use `deleteCard` to **remove a stored credit card** from a customer’s Super Wallet account. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

This request permanently deletes the associated `subscriptionToken` from the customer’s saved payment methods. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

> Common use: allow customers to manage or remove expired or unwanted payment cards from their Super Wallet profile. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Field | Type | Req | Description
----- | ---- | --- | -----------
`Request` | string | Yes | Must be `deleteCard`
`CompanyToken` | string | Yes | Token provided by DPO to authorize API operations
`customerToken` | string | Yes | Customer token retrieved from `createAccount`
`subscriptionToken` | string | Yes | Existing subscription token identifying the card to delete

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>68B90B5E-25F6-4146-8AB1-C7A3A0C41A7F</CompanyToken>
  <Request>deleteCard</Request>
  <customerToken>E6C04D7E-C267-4243-BD1C-49170F8A008B</customerToken>
  <subscriptionToken>65F91D6E-E8A9-4BDA-9481-35432F581F3E</subscriptionToken>
</API3G>
```

> Use this request when a card expires, is replaced, or the customer wishes to revoke authorization. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Response
--------

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Card been deleted</ResultExplanation>
</API3G>
```

Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Field | Type | Description
----- | ---- | -----------
`Result` | integer | Response code returned by the API
`ResultExplanation` | string | Description of the operation result

Result Codes
------------

Code | ResultExplanation | Meaning / Action
---- | ----------------- | ----------------
`000` | Card been deleted | Card deleted successfully
`803` | Invalid or missing `Request` name | Ensure `deleteCard`
`888` | System error | Retry or contact support
`902` | Data mismatch | Verify `customerToken` and `subscriptionToken`
`950` | Missing mandatory fields | Check XML for missing tags
`991` | Encrypted string empty | Request formatting issue
`999` | Customer not found | Ensure valid Super Wallet account  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Typical Usage Flow
------------------

1. Merchant → DPO API: `deleteCard` (CompanyToken, customerToken, subscriptionToken).  
2. DPO API → Merchant: `Result=000` + `ResultExplanation=Card been deleted`.  
3. Merchant: remove card reference from stored customer options. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Notes & Best Practices
----------------------

- **Permanent deletion:** Once deleted, the `subscriptionToken` cannot be reused — a new card must be added via `addCard`.  
- **Customer control:** Ideal for “Manage Payment Methods” or “Delete Card” features in your merchant portal.  
- **Security:** Tokens act as payment credentials; ensure deletion requests are authenticated and authorized.  
- **Error handling:**  
  - `000` → Success — card deleted.  
  - `999` → Customer or card not found — confirm tokens.  
  - `950` → Missing fields — review XML structure.  
- **Compliance:** Always ensure deletions are initiated by the customer or via a verified admin process. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Updated: 5 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super-wallet-delete-card)

Overview – Merchant Operations

The **Merchant Operations** APIs provide access to operational services related to merchant configuration and available payment capabilities. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/merchant-operations-overview)

These endpoints are typically used to retrieve system-level information that supports integration setup, validation, and feature discovery before processing transactions. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/merchant-operations-overview)

- Query available services and payment options

***

Get Services
============

Use `getServices` to retrieve the list of **services** configured on your merchant (e.g., “Safari Holiday”, “Excursion”). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

These `ServiceID` / `ServiceName` pairs are referenced in transaction requests (for example, as `ServiceType` in `createToken`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Field | Req | Description
----- | --- | -----------
`Request` | Yes | Must be `getServices`
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Request>getServices</Request>
</API3G>
```

Response
--------

On success, returns a list of services. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Services>
    <Service>
      <ServiceID>33</ServiceID>
      <ServiceName>Safari Holiday</ServiceName>
    </Service>
    <Service>
      <ServiceID>39</ServiceID>
      <ServiceName>Excursion</ServiceName>
    </Service>
  </Services>
</API3G>
```

Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Field | Description
----- | -----------
`Services/Service` | Repeated list item for each configured service
`ServiceID` | Numeric identifier you pass as `ServiceType` in transaction requests
`ServiceName` | Human-friendly name for UI / reporting

How It’s Used
-------------

- In **Create Token** and related calls, include your chosen service as `ServiceType` using the `ServiceID` value. Example fragment: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

```xml
<Booking>
  <ServiceType>33</ServiceType>
  <Description>Safari Holiday</Description>
  <Date>2025/12/20 19:00</Date>
</Booking>
```

- Use `getServices` to **populate dropdowns** or validate `ServiceType` values at runtime or during setup. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Errors (common)
---------------

Code | Meaning | Action
---- | ------- | ------
`801` | Missing `CompanyToken` | Include valid merchant token
`803` | Invalid/missing `Request` name | Ensure `Request=getServices`
`804` | Error in XML | Check tag names and encoding  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

> Some tenants only document `801`, but standard v6 behaviour may also include `803`/`804` for malformed requests. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Best Practices
--------------

- **Cache** results (e.g., 15–60 minutes) — services list changes infrequently.  
- Store both `ServiceID` and `ServiceName` to display friendly labels in UI and reports.  
- Validate that any `ServiceType` used in transactions **exists** in this list to avoid `902`‑style data mismatch errors in related calls. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Troubleshooting
---------------

Symptom | Likely Cause | Fix
------- | ------------ | ---
Empty list | No services configured | Ask DPO support to configure services
XML error | Wrong casing/encoding | Ensure exact tags & UTF‑8
Using wrong ID in transactions | Mismatch between `ServiceID` and `ServiceType` | Always map `ServiceID` → `ServiceType` 1:1  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

Updated: 5 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/get-services)

***

Overview – xPay Payments

The xPay Payments APIs allow you to initiate xPay transactions and retrieve available balances by currency, enabling programmatic payment execution within the xPay Network. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

xPay Payments
-------------

Use the **xPay Payments** APIs to manage transactions within the xPay Network, including: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

- Opening a new xPay transaction (**Execute xPay**)  
- Retrieving your available balance per currency (**Get Balance**) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

These endpoints are typically used by platforms that need to initiate xPay payments programmatically and confirm available funds before executing or settling transactions. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

Start Here — API Collection
---------------------------

For a complete, interactive view of all endpoints, flows, and sample requests, explore the official Transaction Operations API Collection: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

DPO Pay Transaction Operations API Collection  
Explore full API workflows, test calls, and view sample payloads. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

xPay Payments Workflow
----------------------

Use this interactive recipe to execute xPay transactions and retrieve account balances using the DPO Pay v6 API. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

The workflow demonstrates how to: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

- Submit an xPay request  
- Then verify the resulting balance using the same single-endpoint XML interface [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

It’s designed for merchants and platforms that need to: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

- Automate payouts  
- Monitor available funds  
- Integrate xPay operations into production payment flows [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

xPay Payments Workflow – Open Recipe. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

When to use xPay Payments
-------------------------

Use this category when you need to: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

- Initiate an xPay transaction against your **company balance** in a specific **currency** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)
- Check whether sufficient funds are available before initiating a payment or processing an outgoing transaction [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)
- Build operational tooling (dashboards, reconciliations, internal finance flows) that require balance visibility [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

Available operations
--------------------

### Execute xPay

**Purpose:** Opens a new xPay transaction according to your **company balance** and **currency**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

**Typical flow:** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

1. Confirm you have sufficient balance (optional but recommended)  
2. Submit an Execute xPay request to open the transaction  
3. Handle the response and store the transaction reference for tracking/reconciliation [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

**API reference:** Execute xPay (operation: `executeXpay`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

### Get Balance

**Purpose:** Retrieves your available balance for a specific currency. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

**Typical flow:** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

1. Request balance for the required currency  
2. Use the response to validate whether the account can support the transaction amount  
3. Proceed to Execute xPay (or present an error/alternative path if funds are insufficient) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

**API reference:** Get Balance (operation: `getBalance`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

Request and response format
---------------------------

The xPay Payments operations use an **XML request body** (`application/xml`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

In the docs set, the overview is kept lightweight; full schema and examples are provided on the individual API reference pages. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

Suggested callouts: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

- **Authentication:** Use the standard authentication approach defined for the DPO Pay API (same as other v6 endpoints).  
- **Currency handling:** Always specify the intended currency explicitly when checking balance and creating a transaction.  
- **Operational readiness:** Log and store returned transaction references for auditability and reconciliation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

Common implementation patterns
------------------------------

### Pattern A: Balance-first execution (recommended)

1. **Get Balance** for the currency  
2. Validate available funds  
3. **Execute xPay**  
4. Store response references and status [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

### Pattern B: Direct execution (simpler)

1. **Execute xPay**  
2. If unsuccessful due to balance constraints, handle the failure and retry after replenishment (or route to an alternative flow) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

Related reference sections
--------------------------

For supporting implementation details, refer to: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

- **Gateway Response Codes (v6)**  
- **Verify Token Response Codes (v6)** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

Suggested “Next steps” (optional)
---------------------------------

- Start with **Get Balance** to confirm the integration is authenticated and functioning correctly.  
- Move to **Execute xPay** once you can reliably retrieve balances and have confirmed expected currencies are supported. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay-overview)

***

Execute xPay
============

Use `executeXpay` to open a **new xPay transaction** with one or more **allocations** (internal transfers) based on your **company balance and currency**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Typical use: allocate funds to partner/provider sub-accounts for services (e.g., flights/hotels) using your company balance. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

DPO PAY API (V7)  
- DPO Pay API Collection (v7) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
POST `https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Field | Req | Description
----- | --- | -----------
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token
`Request` | Yes | Must be `executeXpay`
`ProviderToken` | Yes | API token identifying the provider context (top-level)
`Allocations/Allocation[]` | Yes | One or more allocation lines (see below)
`VirtualCardRef` | Yes | Optional virtual card reference ID (tenant-specific; may be required depending on config)

Each Allocation [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Field | Req | Description
----- | --- | -----------
`ProviderToken` | Yes | Provider/sub-merchant token for this allocation
`Amount` | Yes | Allocation amount
`Currency` | Yes | ISO currency (e.g. `USD`)
`Service` | Yes | Service ID (use `getServices` to discover)
`Description` | Yes | Allocation memo/description

Example Request (XML)
---------------------

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Request>executeXpay</Request>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <ProviderToken>CA55CE70-770B-4DFC-BBD0-D02117914C5D</ProviderToken>
  <Allocations>
    <Allocation>
      <ProviderToken>DCBD0E43-1AE6-4758-8641-3B7A7D52ABCD</ProviderToken>
      <Amount>2</Amount>
      <Currency>USD</Currency>
      <Service>6264</Service>
      <Description>Payment for flight</Description>
    </Allocation>
    <Allocation>
      <ProviderToken>47DB152F-4A29-44F2-ADE1-3B7A7D52ABCD</ProviderToken>
      <Amount>1</Amount>
      <Currency>USD</Currency>
      <Service>202</Service>
      <Description>Payment for flight</Description>
    </Allocation>
  </Allocations>
</API3G>
```


Response
--------

Example Success (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Result>000</Result>
  <ResultExplanation>Success</ResultExplanation>
  <RequestRef>9FBC03E2-F289-4E9E-A5AE-0191697149A9</RequestRef>
  <Allocations>
    <Allocation>
      <AllocationId>12345</AllocationId>
    </Allocation>
  </Allocations>
</API3G>
```

Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Field | Description
----- | -----------
`Result` | `000` = success (other codes = error, per v6 response codes)
`ResultExplanation` | Human-readable result
`RequestRef` | Reference for the overall xPay request
`Allocations/Allocation/AllocationId` | Identifier for a created allocation (use with `verifyXpay`)

Typical Flow
------------

1. Merchant → DPO API: `executeXpay` (ProviderToken + Allocations\[ \]).  
2. DPO API → Merchant: `Result=000` + `RequestRef` + `AllocationId`(s).  
3. Merchant → DPO API (as needed): `verifyXpay` by `AllocationId` for status.  
4. Merchant: reconcile allocations internally against your own ledgers. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Best Practices
--------------

- Validate each allocation’s **Amount, Currency, Service** before sending.  
- Persist `RequestRef` and each `AllocationId` for **reconciliation** and **status checks** via `verifyXpay`.  
- Use `getServices` to resolve human-readable service names to IDs, and store the mapping.  
- Implement **idempotency**: avoid sending the same set of allocations twice (e.g., hash the allocation list and store per request). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Troubleshooting
---------------

Symptom | Likely Cause | Action
------- | ------------ | ------
Non-`000` result | Missing/invalid field(s) | Verify `Request=executeXpay`, tokens, and allocation tags
Currency mismatch | Allocation currency not allowed | Align currency with provider/company settings
Unknown service | Invalid `Service` ID | Fetch valid IDs via `getServices`
Cannot track status | Missing IDs | Store `RequestRef` and `AllocationId` from the response  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Metadata & Navigation
---------------------

Next: Check Balance [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/execute-xpay)

Here’s the “Check Balance” page content, cleaned for a `.txt` document. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

***

Check Balance
=============

Get Balance
-----------

Use `getBalance` to retrieve your **available company balance** in a **specific currency**, along with the **exchange rate** applied to your account. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

> Common use: check funds before creating **xPay allocations** or bank/mobile payouts. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

Endpoint
--------

HTTP  
`POST https://secure.3gdirectpay.com/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

Headers  

`Content-Type: application/xml; charset=utf-8`  
`Accept: application/xml` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

Request
-------

Required Fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

Field | Req | Description
----- | --- | -----------
`Request` | Yes | Must be `getBalance`
`CompanyToken` | Yes | Your merchant token
`Currency` | Yes | ISO currency code (e.g., `USD`, `KES`, `ZAR`)

Example Request (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <Request>getBalance</Request>
  <CompanyToken>YOUR_COMPANY_TOKEN</CompanyToken>
  <Currency>USD</Currency>
</API3G>
```

Response
--------

Example Success Response (XML) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

```xml
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<API3G>
  <CompanyBalance>100,000</CompanyBalance>
  <ExchangeRate>1</ExchangeRate>
</API3G>
```

Field Reference [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

Field | Description
----- | -----------
`CompanyBalance` | Your **available balance** in the requested currency (format may include thousand separators)
`ExchangeRate` | Account exchange rate used for this currency (string/decimal)

Notes & Best Practices
----------------------

- Request **one currency at a time**. Call again for each additional currency. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)
- Before `executeXpay` or other payouts, validate you have sufficient `CompanyBalance`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)
- Treat the response as **point-in-time**; balances change as new transactions post. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)
- For reporting, store `(timestamp, currency, CompanyBalance, ExchangeRate)`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

Errors (typical)
----------------

Standard v6 behaviours commonly include: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

Code | Meaning | Action
---- | ------- | ------
`801` | Missing `CompanyToken` | Include a valid token
`803` | Bad/missing `Request` name | Ensure `Request=getBalance`
`804` | XML error | Check tag names/encoding
`902` | Data mismatch | Verify `Currency` is supported

Typical Usage with xPay
-----------------------

1. Merchant → DPO API: `getBalance (Currency)`  
2. DPO API → Merchant: `CompanyBalance + ExchangeRate`  
3. Merchant → DPO API: `executeXpay` (allocations within available balance)  
4. DPO API → Merchant: `AllocationId(s) + RequestRef` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

Quick Links
-----------

- Execute xPay (v6)  
- Verify xPay (v6)  
- Get Services (v6) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/check-balance)

Overview – Reference & Codes

This section provides a central reference for **gateway response codes and verification results** returned by the DPO Pay API. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/reference-codes-overview)

Use these references to **interpret transaction outcomes**, **handle errors correctly**, and **build reliable post-payment logic** in your integration. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/reference-codes-overview)

Whether you’re debugging a failed transaction or validating a successful one, these pages explain **what the gateway returned — and what to do next**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/reference-codes-overview)

Available References

1. Gateway Response Codes  
   Complete list of gateway result codes returned during payment processing, including success, pending, and failure scenarios. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/reference-codes-overview)

2. Verify Token Response Codes  
   Response codes returned when verifying a transaction token, used to confirm final payment status and integrity. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/reference-codes-overview)

When to use this section

You’ll typically refer to these pages when you need to: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/reference-codes-overview)

- Interpret **payment outcomes** returned by the gateway  
- Handle **declines, errors, or pending states** correctly  
- Map gateway responses to **user-friendly messages**  
- Confirm **final transaction status** during verification flows [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/reference-codes-overview)

For implementation guidance, first see the relevant **Transaction Operations** or **Transaction Payment Options** pages, then return here to understand the responses. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/reference-codes-overview)

***

Gateway Response Codes
======================

When calling the DPO Pay by Network API, the gateway returns a numeric `Result` and human‑readable `ResultExplanation` value. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

Use these codes to determine next steps in your payment flow. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

> `000` means success. All other codes indicate a validation, configuration, or processing error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

Response Fields
---------------

Field | Description
----- | -----------
`Result` | Numeric response code indicating the outcome
`ResultExplanation` | Text explanation of the result
`TransToken` | Returned when a token is successfully created
`TransRef` | DPO transaction reference (if created)
`notes` | Additional notes (if provided)
`AllocationID` | Returned for xPay allocation payments
`AllocationCode` | Receiver merchant code (xPay allocation)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

Common Response Codes
---------------------

Code | Meaning | Action for Developer
---- | ------- | --------------------
**000** | Transaction created | Proceed → redirect shopper or process next step
**801** | Missing Company Token | Ensure `CompanyToken` is included
**802** | Invalid Company Token | Verify token value / environment
**803** | Missing or invalid `Request` type | Set `createToken` (or correct operation)
**804** | XML formatting error | Ensure valid XML structure & field case
**901** | Field exceeds max length | Trim values (names, refs, descriptions)
**902** | Missing mandatory fields | Check payment + customer fields
**904** | Unsupported currency | Use valid currency for merchant account
**905** | Transaction exceeds limit | Use smaller amount or contact support
**906** | Monthly merchant limit exceeded | Contact DPO Support
**922** | Invalid provider reference | Verify payment provider configuration
**923** | Allocation > PaymentAmount | Check allocation data (xPay only)
**930** | Invalid block payment code | Review merchant configuration
**940** | `CompanyRef` already paid | Treat as duplicate order or display existing status
**950** | Required tag missing | Check body tags match docs exactly
**960** | Tag sent multiple times | Remove duplicate XML fields  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

Best Practices
--------------

- Log `Result` + `ResultExplanation` + `TransRef` (if present).  
- If you get `804` (XML error), validate structure and remove BOM/extra whitespace.  
- For `940` duplicate reference, query status before retrying.  
- For merchant limit codes (`905`, `906`), send customer‑friendly decline messages. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

Related Guides
--------------

Topic | Link
----- | ----
Create Token | `/developers/create-token`
Callback Processing | `/developers/payment-callbacks`
Status Lookup | `/developers/verify-token`
Refund / Void | `/developers/refund-void`  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

Next Step: Verify Token Example
-------------------------------

Most merchants pair this table with polling for final status: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

XML example (simplified):

```xml
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>{{CompanyToken}}</CompanyToken>
  <Request>verifyToken</Request>
  <TransToken>{{TransToken}}</TransToken>
</API3G>
```



Support
-------

If you hit an unclear gateway response, contact DPO Support and include: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

- `TransRef` or `TransToken`  
- `CompanyRef`  
- Full raw XML request (with token masked)  
- Full raw XML response  
- Timestamp and environment [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/gateway-response-codes)

***

Verify Token Response Codes
===========================

The `verifyToken` API returns a **different set of status codes** than standard gateway responses. Use this table **only** for interpreting results from the `verifyToken` request. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

> This applies when confirming payment status after token creation (e.g., webhook failed, reconciliation, status polling). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

Result Codes
------------

Code | Meaning
---- | -------
**000** | Transaction paid
**001** | Authorized (not yet captured/settled)
**002** | Overpaid / underpaid
**003** | Pending at bank
**005** | Queued for authorization
**007** | Partially paid / split payment pending
**800–899** | Reserved for platform use
**801** | Missing CompanyToken
**802** | CompanyToken does not exist
**803** | Invalid request name
**804** | XML error
**900** | Transaction **not yet paid**
**901** | Transaction declined
**902** | Data mismatch — field provided in explanation
**903** | Payment time limit exceeded
**904** | Transaction cancelled
**950** | Missing mandatory field(s) — field name included  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

Key Response Fields
-------------------

Field | Description
----- | -----------
`Result` | Status code (see table above)
`ResultExplanation` | Human-readable message
`CustomerName` | Shopper name (returned if paid/failed)
`CustomerCredit` | Last 4 digits of card
`CustomerCreditType` | Card type
`TransactionApproval` | Approval number (if paid)
`TransactionCurrency` | Final charged currency
`TransactionAmount` | Amount paid
`TransactionNetAmount` | Net amount after fees
`TransactionSettlementDate` | Settlement date
`TransactionRollingReserveAmount` | Reserve held
`TransactionRollingReserveDate` | Reserve release date
`FraudAlert` | Fraud status indicator (see table below)
`FraudExplanation` | Fraud detail / reason
`CustomerPhone` | Phone
`CustomerCountry` | Country
`CustomerAddress` | Street address
`CustomerCity` | City
`CustomerZip` | Postal code
`MobilePaymentRequest` | Mobile money status
`AccRef` | Internal accounting reference  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

> Not all fields return for all states (e.g. only paid/failed return customer info). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

Fraud Codes
-----------

Code | Meaning
---- | -------
**000** | Genuine transaction
**001** | Low risk (not checked)
**002** | Suspected fraud
**003** | Fraud cleared (merchant manually cleared)
**004** | Suspect fraud alert
**005** | Fraud cleared (system)
**006** | Blacklisted / confirmed fraud  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

Notes
-----

- A result of **900** means the payment **hasn't happened yet** — not an error.  
- `001` means **authorized but not yet captured**.  
- `002` is rare — customer paid a different amount.  
- If callback fails, the system may email the merchant after ~30 minutes (DPO’s fraud/monitoring logic). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

Developer Tip
-------------

Use this to interpret `verifyToken`: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

If Result | Then…
--------- | ------
`000` | Mark as paid
`001` | Await settlement / capture
`900` | Pending — retry later
`901` | Decline — retry allowed
`903` | Token expired — re-initiate checkout
`904` | User canceled checkout
`002` | Flag for manual review (amount mismatch)  [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

Recommended Usage
-----------------

- Poll only if **webhook fails**.  
- Log all `verifyToken` responses for audit.  
- Compare `CompanyRef`, `Amount`, `Currency` to your DB before marking paid. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

Updated: 3 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/verify-token-response-codes)

***

Missing Company Token
=====================

The **“Missing Company Token”** error occurs when your request does not include the required `CompanyToken` credential needed to authenticate or identify your integration. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

You may see variants such as: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

- `request missing company token`  
- `company token not provided`  
- `missing company token in request`  

What this means
---------------

Your API request is being sent **without** the required `CompanyToken`, or the token is not included in the **correct location or format**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

Why this happens
----------------

Typical causes: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

- The `CompanyToken` field is completely missing from the request  
- The token is in the wrong part of the XML/JSON structure  
- The token value is incorrect or incomplete  
- You’re using the wrong token for the environment (test vs live)  

How to fix it
-------------

### 1. Ensure the CompanyToken is included

Verify your request contains the `CompanyToken` parameter. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

Example (XML skeleton): [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

```xml
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>your_company_token_here</CompanyToken>
  ...
</API3G>
```

### 2. Place it in the correct location

Include `CompanyToken` in the **root body** exactly where the specific endpoint’s docs show it. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

Check the request structure for the API you’re calling (e.g. `createToken`, `chargeTokenMobile`, `getBalance`, etc.). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

### 3. Verify your token value

- Copy/paste carefully — no leading/trailing spaces.  
- Confirm the token belongs to the correct merchant account.  
- Ensure you are using the **sandbox** token in sandbox and the **live** token in production. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

### 4. Confirm you actually received a Company Token

The Company Token is issued during onboarding. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

- Check onboarding emails from DPO Pay / Network.  
- If you cannot find it, contact DPO Pay support to request or reissue it. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

Example
-------

❌ Incorrect request (missing `CompanyToken`): [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

```xml
<API3G>
  <Request>createToken</Request>
  <!-- CompanyToken is missing here -->
  ...
</API3G>
```

✅ Correct request (with `CompanyToken`): [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

```xml
<API3G>
  <CompanyToken>your_company_token_here</CompanyToken>
  <Request>createToken</Request>
  ...
</API3G>
```

Related errors
--------------

You may also encounter: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

- **Invalid Company Token**  
- **Company Token does not exist**  
- **Invalid or missing request type**  

Need help?
----------

If the error persists: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

- Compare your request to the official API examples for that endpoint.  
- Confirm your credentials with your integration/onboarding team.  
- Contact DPO Pay support with your sample request/response for assistance.  

By ensuring `CompanyToken` is present, valid, and correctly placed, you can resolve the **“Missing Company Token”** error and continue your integration. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/missing-company-token-request-missing-company-token-error)

Plugins – Overview
==================

Integrate DPO Pay with popular ecommerce platforms. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)

DPO Pay provides ready-made plugins so you can add payment capabilities to common shopping carts and store builders with minimal custom development. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)

Instead of building a full custom integration, you install and configure a module that connects your store directly to DPO Pay. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)

What you’ll need (quick checklist)
----------------------------------

To use any plugin, you typically need: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)

- An active DPO Pay merchant account (sandbox or live)  
- API credentials from the DPO Pay Merchant Portal  
- Access to your ecommerce platform admin area  
- Basic configuration details (merchant ID, keys, endpoints)  

Available platform plugins
--------------------------

Each link points to a dedicated setup/configuration guide. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)

- WooCommerce – Install and configure the DPO Pay plugin for WooCommerce stores. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- Shopify – Integration options for accepting payments on Shopify. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- PrestaShop – Module setup and configuration for PrestaShop. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- Wix – Options for enabling DPO Pay on Wix websites. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- Magento 2 – Adobe Commerce / Magento plugin installation guide. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- Gravity Forms – Accept payments via WordPress Gravity Forms. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- Ecwid – Configure DPO Pay for Ecwid online stores. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- OpenCart – Payment module setup for OpenCart platforms. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- nopCommerce – .NET ecommerce plugin configuration (v4.6.0). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- WHMCS – Billing platform gateway integration steps. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)
- Odoo – Payment provider configuration for Odoo ERP. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/plugins-overview)

Navigation context

Shopify – DPO Pay Plugin
========================

Accept payments on Shopify with DPO Pay  

The DPO Pay Shopify app allows merchants to securely accept local and international payments directly from their Shopify store using the DPO Pay platform. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

This plugin connects your Shopify checkout to DPO Pay, providing a hosted, secure payment experience without custom development. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

Overview
--------

With the DPO Pay Shopify integration you can: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Accept credit and debit card payments  
- Support multiple payment methods across Africa  
- Process local and cross-border transactions  
- Provide a secure hosted checkout experience  
- Manage payments through your existing DPO Pay merchant account  

The plugin is free to install; standard DPO Pay transaction fees apply. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

Install on Shopify: https://apps.shopify.com/dpo-group [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

What You’ll Need
----------------

Before installing the plugin, you should have: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

- An active DPO Pay merchant account (sandbox or live)  
- Your DPO Pay API credentials  
- Access to your Shopify store admin panel  
- Basic store configuration completed in Shopify  

If you don’t have a DPO Pay account yet, contact the DPO Pay onboarding team. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

Installation Guide
------------------

### Step 1 – Install the App

1. Log in to your Shopify admin panel.  
2. Go to the Shopify App Store.  
3. Search for “DPO Pay”.  
4. Click “Install App”.  

After installation, the DPO Pay configuration screen appears in your Shopify dashboard. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Step 2 – Configure Your Credentials

1. Open the DPO Pay app in your Shopify admin.  
2. Enter your merchant details and API credentials.  
3. Select the environment: Sandbox or Live.  
4. Save the configuration.  

Your Shopify store is now connected to DPO Pay. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Step 3 – Enable the Payment Method

1. In Shopify, go to Settings → Payments.  
2. Find DPO Pay under available payment providers.  
3. Activate the gateway.  
4. Save your changes.  

DPO Pay will now show as a payment option at checkout. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

Customer Experience
-------------------

Once enabled, the checkout flow is: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

1. **Create Order** – Customer adds items to cart and goes to checkout.  
2. **Select Payment Method** – Customer chooses DPO Pay at the payment step.  
3. **Complete Payment** – Customer is redirected to the secure DPO Pay payment page to finish payment.  
4. **Order Confirmation** – After success, customer is returned to Shopify and sees a confirmed order status.  

Supported Features
------------------

- Secure hosted payment page  
- Multiple payment methods  
- Transaction status updates  
- Order confirmation handling  
- Support for refunds via Shopify admin  
- Compatible with standard Shopify checkout [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

Troubleshooting
---------------

### Payments not appearing in Shopify

- Verify API credentials.  
- Ensure the correct environment (Sandbox or Live) is selected.  
- Confirm DPO Pay is enabled in Shopify payment settings. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

### DPO Pay not visible at checkout

- Check that the gateway is activated.  
- Confirm currency and region settings in Shopify.  
- Ensure test mode is disabled for live transactions. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

Frequently Asked Questions
--------------------------

**Is the plugin free?**  
Yes. The Shopify app is free to install; standard DPO Pay processing fees apply. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

**Which countries are supported?**  
DPO Pay supports multiple African markets and international card payments. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

**Can I test before going live?**  
Yes. Use your DPO Pay sandbox credentials for test transactions. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

Support
-------

For help with the plugin: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

- DPO Pay Support: support@dpogroup.com  
- Developer Documentation: DPO Pay API Docs  

Updated: 2 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/shopify-dpo-pay-plugin)

WooCommerce – DPO Pay Plugin
============================

Accept online payments in WooCommerce using DPO Pay. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

The DPO Pay plugin for WooCommerce lets you accept online payments directly from your WooCommerce store, including credit and debit cards, digital wallets, and other methods supported by DPO Pay. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

This official plugin connects your WooCommerce checkout to the secure DPO Pay payment platform, giving your customers a simple, trusted way to pay. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

Why Choose DPO Pay?
-------------------

DPO Pay provides a secure checkout experience with: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Local and international card payments  
- Multiple African payment methods  
- Secure hosted payment processing  
- Reliable transaction management  
- Advanced fraud protection [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

Download the Plugin
-------------------

You can download the latest WooCommerce plugin as `dpo-group-for-woocommerce.zip`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

Installation Guide
------------------

### Step 1 – Install the Plugin

1. Log in to your WordPress admin dashboard.  
2. Go to **Plugins → Add New**.  
3. Click **Upload Plugin**.  
4. Upload `dpo-group-for-woocommerce.zip`.  
5. Click **Install Now**.  
6. After installation, click **Activate**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

Configuration Guide
-------------------

### Enable the Payment Gateway

1. In WordPress, go to **WooCommerce → Settings → Payments**.  
2. Find **DPO Group** in the payment methods list.  
3. Toggle to **Enabled**.  
4. Click **Manage**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Primary Settings

On the DPO Group settings page: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Enable **DPO Group Gateway**.  
- Set the Title and Description shown to customers.  
- Enter your **Company Token** (from DPO Pay).  

The Company Token connects the plugin to your DPO Pay merchant account. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Additional Settings

Advanced options include: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Default DPO Service Type (optional)  
- Enable Test Mode (sandbox)  
- Enable Logging (recommended for troubleshooting)  
- DPO Group API URL (do not change)  
- DPO Pay URL (do not change)  
- PTL Type (Minutes/Hours)  
- PTL (payment time limit)  
- Successful Order Status (e.g., Processing)  
- Optional order metadata settings  

Click **Save changes** after configuring. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

Product-Level Configuration
---------------------------

For service-based products you can set a per-product **DPO Service Type**: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

1. Edit a product in WooCommerce.  
2. In **Product Data**, open **DPO Service Type**.  
3. Enter the required service type code if needed. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

Customer Payment Flow
---------------------

1. Customer adds items to cart.  
2. At checkout they choose **DPO Group** as payment method.  
3. They’re redirected to the secure DPO Pay hosted payment page.  
4. After payment, they return to WooCommerce with a confirmed order.  

No coding is required. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

FAQ
***

**Do I need a DPO Pay merchant account?**  
Yes. You need a DPO Pay account and a **Company Token**. Sign up at `dpogroup.com/get-started/` or email `sales1@dpogroup.com`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

**Do I need SSL?**  
An SSL certificate is recommended for shopper security. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

**Where is the API documentation?**  
See the DPO Pay developer portal and user guide for plugin setup details. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

**Who can help me configure it?**  
DPO Pay Support: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Email: `support@dpogroup.com`  
- Phone: `+254 (0) 709 947947`  

Troubleshooting Tips
--------------------

- Ensure your **Company Token** is correct.  
- Check Test Mode vs Live Mode.  
- Don’t change default API URLs.  
- Enable logging if transactions don’t complete.  
- Verify your merchant account is active/enabled. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

Updated: 2 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/woocommerce-dpo-pay-plugin)

PrestaShop – DPO Pay Plugin
===========================

Accept payments in PrestaShop using DPO Pay  

The DPO Pay plugin for PrestaShop allows merchants to securely accept online payments directly from their PrestaShop store using the DPO Pay platform. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

This official module integrates your checkout with DPO Pay’s hosted payment gateway, giving customers access to a wide range of local and international payment methods with minimal setup. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

Why Use the DPO Pay PrestaShop Plugin?
--------------------------------------

With the DPO Pay PrestaShop module you can: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Accept credit and debit card payments  
- Support multiple African and global payment methods  
- Process secure hosted payments  
- Offer customers a seamless checkout experience  
- Manage transactions through your DPO Pay merchant account  

Pricing: the plugin is free to install; standard DPO Pay transaction fees apply. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

Download the Plugin
-------------------

The latest version of the PrestaShop module can be downloaded from the official DPO Pay GitHub repository: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Download PrestaShop Plugin: https://github.com/DPO-Group/DPO_PrestaShop

Installation Guide
------------------

### Step 1 – Download the Plugin

1. Visit: https://github.com/DPO-Group/DPO_PrestaShop  
2. Go to the **Releases** section.  
3. Download the latest plugin package (e.g., `dpo.zip`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Step 2 – Install the Plugin in PrestaShop

1. Log in to your **PrestaShop admin panel**.  
2. From the left-hand menu, open: **Improve → Modules → Module Manager**.  
3. Click **Upload a Module**.  
4. Select the downloaded `dpo.zip` file.  
5. Wait for the installation confirmation message.  
6. Click **Configure** once installation is complete. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Step 3 – Configure the Plugin

After installation: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

1. Locate the **DPO Pay module** under **Installed Modules**.  
2. Click **Configure**.  
3. Enter your DPO Pay merchant credentials and required settings.  
4. Save the configuration.  

Your store is now connected to DPO Pay and ready to accept payments. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

What You’ll Need
----------------

Before configuring the module, ensure you have: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

- An active DPO Pay merchant account  
- Your DPO Pay credentials and integration details  
- Access to your PrestaShop admin dashboard  

If you do not yet have a DPO Pay account, contact the DPO Pay onboarding team. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

Customer Payment Flow
---------------------

Once the module is installed and configured: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

1. Customer adds products to their cart.  
2. At checkout, they select **DPO Pay** as the payment method.  
3. They are redirected to the secure DPO Pay hosted payment page.  
4. After payment, they are returned to PrestaShop with an updated order status.  

No custom coding is required. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

Frequently Asked Questions
--------------------------

### Does this require a DPO Pay merchant account?

Yes. You must have an active DPO Pay account and merchant credentials to use this plugin. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Is an SSL certificate required?

Using an SSL certificate on your PrestaShop store is strongly recommended for secure communication and to protect customer data. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Is the plugin free?

Yes. The module is free to download and install; normal DPO Pay processing fees apply. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Who can help if I need support?

Contact the DPO Pay Support Team: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Email: support@dpogroup.com  
- Website: https://dpogroup.com/

Troubleshooting Tips
--------------------

If payments are not processing correctly: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Confirm your merchant credentials are entered correctly.  
- Ensure the module is enabled in PrestaShop.  
- Verify that your DPO Pay account is active.  
- Check that your store is using HTTPS.  
- Review any error messages shown in the PrestaShop logs.  

Plugin Details
--------------

- Developer: DPO Group  
- Platform: PrestaShop  
- Current Version: v1.2.0 (for PrestaShop v8.2.1)  
- Language: English  
- Category: Payment Gateway  

Updated: 2 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/prestashop-dpo-pay-plugin)

Wix – DPO Pay Integration
=========================

Accept payments on Wix using DPO Pay  

Wix merchants can connect **DPO Group (DPO Pay)** as a payment provider directly within Wix. This lets you accept credit, debit and prepaid card payments, plus mobile money options across Africa, without installing a custom plugin. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

Why use DPO Pay with Wix
------------------------

By connecting DPO Pay to your Wix store, you can: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

- Accept local and international card payments  
- Offer mobile money options (M-Pesa, Airtel, Tigo, MTN, Vodafone, etc.)  
- Process secure online transactions through DPO Pay  
- Support customers across multiple African countries  
- Manage payments and payouts via your DPO Pay merchant account  

Supported countries (examples): Ethiopia, Uganda, Rwanda, Kenya, Tanzania, Malawi, Zimbabwe, Mauritius, Zambia, Botswana, Namibia, DRC, Nigeria, Ghana, Ivory Coast, South Africa, Eswatini (Swaziland), Tunisia. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

Currencies: all are supported, but **Wix store currency must match your DPO Pay account currency**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

What you’ll need
----------------

Before connecting: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

- Active **DPO Pay merchant account**  
- **Company Token** and **Service Type** from DPO Pay  
- Access to your Wix dashboard  

Signup: https://dpogroup.com/get-started/ [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

How to connect DPO Pay in Wix
-----------------------------

### Step 1 – Open Payment Settings

1. Log in to your Wix dashboard  
2. Go to **Accept Payments**  
3. Confirm your **business location** (top‑right); correct it if needed [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

### Step 2 – Select DPO Group as a provider

1. Click **See More Payment Options**  
2. Find **DPO Group** in the providers list  
3. Click **Connect** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

### Step 3 – Connect your account

If you already have a DPO Pay account: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

1. Enter your **Company Token** and **Service Type**  
2. Click **Connect**  

If you don’t yet have an account: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

1. Click **Create DPO Group Account**  
2. Complete onboarding  
3. Wait for the email with **Company Token** and **Service Type**  
4. Return to Wix and connect using those details  

Support email for tokens/details: **support@dpogroup.com**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

### Step 4 – Start accepting payments

Once connected: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

- DPO Pay appears as a payment method at checkout  
- Customers can pay with cards and supported mobile methods  
- Transactions are processed securely through DPO Pay  

No extra plugin/config inside Wix is required. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

Important notes
---------------

**Currency matching**  
- Wix store currency must match DPO Pay account currency; otherwise transactions may be declined. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

**Minimum amounts**  
- Some providers enforce minimum transaction amounts (e.g., USD 1.01). Ensure product prices are above any minimum. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

**Recurring payments**  
- Recurring billing depends on provider support; ensure the chosen provider supports subscriptions if needed. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

**Payouts**  
- Payouts, refunds and chargebacks are managed directly by DPO Pay support. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

FAQ
***

How to contact DPO Group?  
- Website: https://dpogroup.com  
- Phone: +254 709 947947  
- Email: support@dpogroup.com [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

Can I create discounts/coupons via DPO Pay?  
- No. Create discounts/coupons in Wix, not in DPO Pay. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

How to check if DPO Pay is active?  
- Account verified  
- DPO Pay visible at checkout  
- Test transactions succeed [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

What if my currency is not supported?  
- Change Wix currency or contact DPO Pay for guidance. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

Support
-------

- **DPO Pay:** support@dpogroup.com  
- **Wix Help Center:** https://support.wix.com  
- **Official Wix guide:** https://support.wix.com/en/article/connecting-dpo-group-as-a-payment-provider [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

Integration details
-------------------

- Platform: Wix  
- Integration type: Native payment provider (no plugin needed)  
- Developer: DPO Group  
- Pricing: Free to connect (standard DPO Pay processing fees apply) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/wix-dpo-pay-integration)

Here’s the “Magento 2 – DPO Pay Plugin” page content, cleaned for a `.txt` document. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

Magento 2 – DPO Pay Plugin
==========================

Accept payments in Magento 2 using DPO Pay  

The **DPO Pay Magento 2 plugin** enables merchants to accept secure online payments directly from their Magento 2 stores using the DPO Pay platform. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

The module integrates Magento checkout with DPO Pay’s hosted payment gateway, allowing customers to pay with cards and other supported payment methods across Africa and beyond. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

Why Use the DPO Pay Magento Plugin?
-----------------------------------

By installing the DPO Pay module for Magento 2, you can: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Accept credit and debit card payments  
- Support multiple African payment methods  
- Process secure hosted payments  
- Offer customers a trusted checkout experience  
- Manage transactions through your DPO Pay merchant account  

The plugin is free to install; standard DPO Pay transaction fees apply. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

Download the Plugin
-------------------

The latest version of the Magento 2 plugin is available from the official DPO Pay GitHub repository: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Download Magento Plugin: https://github.com/DPO-Group/DPO_Magento_2

What You’ll Need
----------------

Before installing the module, ensure you have: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

- An active **DPO Pay merchant account**  
- Merchant credentials and configuration details  
- Access to your Magento 2 admin panel  
- Command-line (SSH) access to your Magento server  

If you do not yet have a DPO Pay account, visit: https://dpogroup.com/get-started/ [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

Installation Guide
------------------

The DPO Pay Magento 2 module can be installed in two ways: via Composer (recommended) or manually. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Option 1 – Automatic Installation (Composer) – Recommended

Run the following Composer command in your Magento root: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

```bash
composer require dpo/dpo-gateway
```

Then follow the Magento CLI steps below. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Option 2 – Manual Installation

1. Open the **Releases** section of the GitHub repository.  
2. Download the latest `Dpo.zip` package.  
3. Extract the ZIP locally.  
4. Upload the extracted `Dpo` directory into: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

```bash
/app/code/
```



Magento CLI Commands
--------------------

After installing the files (via Composer or manually), run these commands from the Magento root: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

```bash
composer require dpo/dpo-pay-common:1.0.2
php bin/magento module:enable Dpo_Dpo
php bin/magento setup:upgrade
php bin/magento setup:di:compile
php bin/magento setup:static-content:deploy
php bin/magento indexer:reindex
php bin/magento cache:clean
```

These commands enable the module and register the payment method in Magento. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

Configuration Guide
-------------------

After installation: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

1. Log in to the **Magento Admin Panel**.  
2. Go to: **Stores → Configuration → Sales → Payment Methods → DPO Pay**.  
3. Find **DPO Pay** in the payment methods list.  
4. Enter your DPO Pay merchant credentials and required settings.  
5. Configure options according to your business needs.  
6. Click **Save Config**.  

DPO Pay will now be available as a payment option at checkout. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

Customer Payment Flow
---------------------

Once configured: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

1. Customer adds products to cart.  
2. At checkout they select **DPO Pay** as the payment method.  
3. They are redirected to the secure DPO Pay hosted payment page.  
4. After successful payment, they are returned to Magento with updated order status.  

No additional coding is required. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

Frequently Asked Questions
--------------------------

### Is a DPO Pay merchant account required?

Yes. An active DPO Pay merchant account and credentials are required to configure this module. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Is the plugin free?

Yes. The Magento 2 plugin is free to download and install; standard DPO Pay processing fees apply. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Do I need an SSL certificate?

Yes. Magento stores processing payments should always use HTTPS and a valid SSL certificate. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

### Who can help if I need support?

Contact the DPO Pay Support Team: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Email: support@dpogroup.com  
- Website: https://dpogroup.com/

Troubleshooting Tips
--------------------

If you experience issues after installation: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/magento-2-dpo-pay-plugin)

- Confirm all Magento CLI commands completed successfully.  
- Verify the module is enabled in Magento configuration.  
- Ensure merchant credentials are correct.  
- Clear Magento cache after configuration changes.  
- Confirm your DPO Pay account is active and correctly configured.

DPO Pay for Gravity Forms
=========================

DPO Pay plugin v1.2.0 for Gravity Forms v2.9.10  

The **DPO Pay Gravity Forms plugin** lets you accept secure online payments directly from Gravity Forms on your WordPress website, supporting cards, digital wallets, and other DPO Pay methods. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

Download
--------

Download from GitHub: **gravity-forms-dpo-group-plugin.zip**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

Repository: https://github.com/DPO-Group/DPO_Gravity_Forms [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

Installation
------------

### Step 1 – Download the Plugin

1. Visit the GitHub releases page.  
2. Download the latest release: `gravity-forms-dpo-group-plugin.zip`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

### Step 2 – Install the Plugin

1. Log in to **WordPress Admin**.  
2. Go to **Plugins → Add New → Upload Plugin**.  
3. Choose the ZIP file and click **Install Now**.  
4. Click **Activate Plugin** after installation. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

Configuration
-------------

### Step 3 – Configure the DPO Pay Feed

1. In WordPress, click **Forms**.  
2. Select the Gravity Form to connect.  
3. Open **Form Settings → DPO Pay**.  
4. Under **DPO Pay Feeds**, click **Add New**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

### Configure Feed Settings

- Set **Transaction Type** to **Products and Services**.  
- Map Gravity Forms fields to DPO Pay fields:  
  - Email  
  - Country  
  - Address (if applicable)  
  - Pricing fields [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

Important: Your form must include: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

- At least one **Pricing Field**  
- An **Email Field**  
- A **Country Field**  

Then **Save Settings**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

### Step 4 – Configure Confirmation Messages

To handle transaction outcomes: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

1. Go to **Form Settings → Confirmations**.  
2. Create three confirmations:

- **approved** – message: “Transaction Approved”  
- **cancelled** – message: “Transaction Cancelled”  
- **failed** – message: “Transaction Failed”  

DPO Pay uses these to redirect users according to the payment result. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

Testing
-------

Before going live: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

- Enable **Test Mode** in the DPO Pay feed.  
- Run a test transaction.  
- Verify:  
  - Redirects work  
  - Correct confirmation messages show  
  - Email notifications fire  

Then switch to **Production** mode. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

Support & Collaboration
-----------------------

- Support: **support@dpogroup.com** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)
- Contributions: submit PRs via the GitHub repo. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)

Updated: 2 months ago. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-gravity-forms)
