DPO Pay for Ecwid
=================

Accept payments in Ecwid using DPO Pay  

The DPO Pay integration for Ecwid enables you to accept secure online payments directly from your Ecwid store. Customers can pay using credit and debit cards, mobile money, and other payment methods supported by DPO Pay. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

If you need assistance, contact **support@dpogroup.com**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

Overview
--------

With DPO Pay connected to Ecwid, you can: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

- Accept online card payments securely  
- Offer mobile money options across Africa  
- Process cross-border payments  
- Settle in multiple currencies  
- Manage payouts through your DPO Pay merchant account  

This integration is managed from the **Ecwid App Market** and requires **no coding**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

Supported Features
------------------

- All major credit and debit cards  
- Mobile money payments (M-Pesa, Airtel, Tigo, MTN, Vodafone – where supported)  
- Multi-currency processing  
- Secure hosted payment pages  
- Real-time transaction processing [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

Installation and Setup
----------------------

### Step 1 – Install the DPO Pay App

1. Log in to your **Ecwid Admin Panel**.  
2. Go to **Apps → App Market**.  
3. Search for **DPO Group**.  
4. Select the **DPO Group** payment app.  
5. Click **Install**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

### Step 2 – Connect Your DPO Pay Account

After installation: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

1. Open the installed **DPO Group** app in Ecwid.  
2. Click **Connect**.  
3. Enter the credentials provided by DPO Pay:  
   - **Company Token**  
   - **Service Type**  
4. Save your settings. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

If you do not yet have a DPO Pay account, you’ll be guided through onboarding. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

Requirements
------------

You need: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

- An active Ecwid store  
- A DPO Pay merchant account  
- Your **Company Token** and **Service Type** from DPO Pay  

If you don’t have these, email **support@dpogroup.com**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

Video Installation Guide
------------------------

A step-by-step video is available on YouTube: **“How to Set Up DPO Group for Ecwid”**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

Watch here: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=S7oeKyO6myA [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

The video covers: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

- Installing from the Ecwid App Market  
- Connecting your DPO Pay account  
- Configuring payment options  
- Testing the integration  

Frequently Asked Questions
--------------------------

### Which countries are supported?

DPO Pay supports merchants across Africa, including: Ethiopia, Uganda, Rwanda, Kenya, Tanzania, Malawi, Zimbabwe, Mauritius, Zambia, Botswana, Namibia, DRC, Nigeria, Ghana, Ivory Coast, South Africa, Swaziland/Eswatini, Tunisia, and more. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

### Which currencies are accepted?

All currencies supported by DPO Pay can be processed via Ecwid. Ensure your Ecwid store currency matches your DPO Pay account currency. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

### How do payouts work?

Payouts and settlements are managed via your DPO Pay merchant account. For payout schedules and reconciliation, contact DPO Pay support. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

### Who can I contact for help?

- Email: **support@dpogroup.com**  
- Website: https://www.dpogroup.com/ [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-ecwid)

--------------------

DPO Pay for OpenCart
====================

DPO Pay plugin v1.2.0 for OpenCart v4.1.0.0  

The **DPO Pay plugin for OpenCart** allows merchants to accept secure online payments directly from their OpenCart store using the DPO Pay payment gateway. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

You can accept credit and debit cards, mobile money, and other supported payment methods across Africa and internationally. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

If you need assistance, contact **support@dpogroup.com**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

Features
--------

- Secure payment processing via DPO Pay  
- Support for multiple payment methods  
- Easy installation and configuration  
- Seamless checkout experience  
- Compatible with OpenCart version 4.1.0.0  
- Support for multiple currencies [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

Requirements
------------

Before installing the plugin, ensure that you have: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

- An active **DPO Pay merchant account**  
- Your **Company Token** and **Service Type** from DPO Pay  
- Access to your OpenCart admin panel  

If you don’t yet have a DPO Pay account, sign up at: https://dpogroup.com/get-started/ [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

Installation Guide
------------------

Follow these steps to install and configure the plugin. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

### 1. Download the Plugin

- Go to the official GitHub repository: https://github.com/DPO-Group/DPO_OpenCart  
- Download the latest plugin package: **dpo.ocmod.zip** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

### 2. Install the Plugin

1. Log in to your **OpenCart admin panel**.  
2. Navigate to **Extensions → Installer**.  
3. Under **Upload File**, click **Upload**.  
4. Select `dpo.ocmod.zip`.  
5. Click the **Install** button (green plus icon).  

The plugin is now uploaded to OpenCart. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

### 3. Activate the Plugin

1. Go to **Extensions → Extensions**.  
2. In **Choose the extension type**, select **Payments**.  
3. Find **DPO Pay** in the list.  
4. Click the **Install** button (green plus icon). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

### 4. Configure the Plugin

1. Click the **Edit** (blue pencil) icon next to **DPO Pay**.  
2. Enter your DPO Pay credentials:  
   - Company Token  
   - Service Type  
   - Any additional API details if required  
3. Set **Status** to **Enabled**.  
4. Configure your preferred **Order Status** mapping.  
5. Click **Save**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

Your OpenCart store is now ready to process payments via DPO Pay. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

Testing the Integration
-----------------------

Perform test transactions to confirm: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

- Payments are processed correctly  
- Orders update to the correct status  
- Customers are redirected correctly after payment  

If sandbox/test credentials are needed, contact DPO Pay Support. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

Troubleshooting
---------------

If you run into issues: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

- Confirm Company Token and Service Type are accurate.  
- Make sure the plugin **Status** is set to **Enabled**.  
- Verify your OpenCart version is supported.  
- Check your DPO Pay merchant account is active. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

Collaboration
-------------

This plugin is open source. Developers can contribute via pull requests: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

- Repository: https://github.com/DPO-Group/DPO_OpenCart [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

----------

For any questions or support: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-opencart)

- Email: **support@dpogroup.com**  
- Website: https://dpogroup.com/

DPO Pay NopCommerce Plugin (v4.6.0)
===================================

DPO Pay provides a secure and reliable payment integration for **NopCommerce v4.60**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

With this plugin, merchants can accept **credit cards, debit cards, mobile money, and cross-border payments** through DPO’s secure payment platform. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

If you require assistance at any stage, please contact the **DPO Pay support team**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

Compatibility
-------------

- **Plugin Version:** v4.6.0  
- **Supported Platform:** NopCommerce v4.60 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

Installation
------------

1. Navigate to the official GitHub releases page.  
2. Download the latest release (v4.6.0).  
3. Unzip the downloaded file.  
4. Follow the included **Integration Guide PDF** inside the ZIP package. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

> The integration guide contains detailed configuration steps and setup instructions specific to your NopCommerce environment. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

Configuration Overview
----------------------

Once installed: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

1. Log in to your **NopCommerce Admin Panel**.  
2. Go to: `Configuration → Payment Methods`.  
3. Locate **DPO Pay** in the payment methods list.  
4. Click **Configure**.  
5. Enter your:  
   - Company Token  
   - Service Type  
6. Save your configuration.  
7. Ensure the payment method is set to **Active**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

Requirements
------------

You will need: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

- An active **DPO Pay merchant account**  
- **Company Token** and **Service Type** issued by DPO  
- Matching **currency configuration** between your store and your DPO account  

If you do not yet have a merchant account, please contact DPO Pay support. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

Download
--------

You can download or fork the plugin directly from GitHub:  

- **Download NopCommerce Plugin:** https://github.com/DPO-Group/DPO_NopCommerce [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

Collaboration
-------------

Contributions are welcome.  

Please submit pull requests with any enhancements, improvements, or fixes. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

DPO’s highly secure payment platform makes payments simple by allowing businesses to accept **credit cards, mobile payments, and cross-border payments**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

Their mission is to bring African businesses advanced online and offline payment processing technologies while supporting growth and financial inclusion. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-nopcommerce-plugin-v460)

DPO Pay for WHMCS
=================

**DPO Pay WHMCS plugin v1.1.0 for WHMCS v8.11.2** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

The DPO Pay plugin for WHMCS lets you accept secure online payments directly within your WHMCS billing system. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

With DPO Pay for WHMCS, you can: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

- Accept credit and debit card payments  
- Process secure online transactions  
- Redirect customers to DPO’s secure payment page  
- Receive automatic payment confirmations back into WHMCS  

This is ideal for hosting providers, SaaS, and subscription businesses using WHMCS. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

***

Installation
------------

### 1. Download the Plugin [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

1. Go to the **releases page** on GitHub.  
2. Download the latest release (`modules.zip`).  
3. Extract the ZIP file locally.  

### 2. Install the Plugin [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

1. Copy the extracted **modules** folder contents into your WHMCS root directory:

   `whmcsrootfolder/modules/`

2. Ensure the DPO Pay files are under:

   `/modules/gateways/`

### 3. Activate the Plugin [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

1. Log in to the **WHMCS Admin Area**.  
2. Navigate to: `Setup → Apps & Integrations`.  
3. Search for **DPO Pay**.  
4. Click **Activate**.  

### 4. Configure the Plugin [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

After activation, enter:

- **Company Token**  
- **Service Type**  
- Any other required settings  

Then click **Save Changes**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

You get Company Token and Service Type from DPO Pay when your merchant account is created. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

***

Testing
-------

Before going live: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

- Ensure WHMCS is running over HTTPS.  
- Run test transactions with DPO sandbox / test credentials.  
- Confirm successful and failed payments return correctly to WHMCS.  

***

Requirements
------------

- WHMCS v8.11.2 (or compatible)  
- Active DPO Pay merchant account  
- PHP/server compatible with your WHMCS version  
- SSL certificate enabled on your WHMCS domain [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

***

Support
-------

If you run into issues: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

- Email: **support@dpogroup.com**  
- Contact your DPO account manager  
- Check the integration guide included in the GitHub release

-------------

Developers can submit pull requests and improvements via the official GitHub repository. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-for-whmcs)

DPO_Odoo – DPO Pay Odoo Addon
=============================

**DPO Pay Odoo Addon v1.1.1 for Odoo v18.0** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

This is the official **DPO Pay payment addon for Odoo**, allowing you to accept secure online payments through DPO Pay directly from your Odoo website/shop. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

If you need assistance, contact the **DPO Pay support team**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

Installation
------------

### 1. Download the Addon [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

- Go to the **releases page** of the DPO_Odoo repository.  
- Download the latest release: `payment_dpo.zip`.  
- Unzip the file.  

Direct link: **https://github.com/DPO-Group/DPO_Odoo** [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

### 2. Install the Addon [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

1. Upload the extracted `payment_dpo` folder to your Odoo **addons directory**.  
   - Ensure you **supplement** existing files/folders rather than replacing them.  
2. Log in to your Odoo admin area.  
3. Navigate to:

   `Settings → Activate the developer mode`  

4. Then go to:

   `Apps → Update Apps List`  

5. Click **Update**.  
6. Restart your Odoo instance.  

### 3. Configure the Addon [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

1. In the **Apps** search bar, search for **DPO Pay**.  
2. Click **Activate**, then click **Upgrade** if prompted.  
3. Navigate to:

   `Settings → Website → View Alternatives (under Shop → Payment)`  

4. Under **Payment Providers**, click **Activate** for **DPO Pay**.  
5. Enter your DPO Pay credentials and required configuration details (e.g., **Company Token**, mode, etc.).  
6. Click **Save manually**.  
7. Navigate back to:

   `Settings → Deactivate the developer mode`  

8. Restart your Odoo instance again.  

Configuration Notes
-------------------

When configuring DPO Pay in Odoo, ensure: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

- You enter the correct **Company Token** supplied by DPO.  
- Your **Payment Mode** is correctly selected (**Test** or **Production**).  
- Any **return URLs** and **webhook endpoints** are correctly configured (if applicable to your deployment).  

Collaboration
-------------

Developers are encouraged to contribute. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

- Submit pull requests with enhancements, fixes, or new features in the GitHub repo.  

About DPO
---------

DPO’s secure payment platform allows businesses to accept **credit cards, mobile payments, and cross-border payments**, both online and offline. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

The mission is to provide African businesses with advanced payment processing technologies, supporting growth and financial inclusion. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo_odoo)

DPO Pay API (V6) – Overview
===========================

The **DPO Pay API (V6)** provides the core services required to build and manage payment experiences on the DPO Pay platform. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Using this API collection, you can: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

- Create payment tokens and manage transaction lifecycles  
- Retrieve supported payment options for each transaction  
- Integrate **xPay Payments** flows  
- Integrate **Super Wallet** (stored cards, recurring payments)  
- Discover merchant services and capabilities  

API Sections
------------

The V6 API is organized into the following groups: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

1. **Transaction Operations** – Core payment operations: create tokens, verify tokens, refund/void, update, email payment links, verify xPay, generate mVisa QR.  
2. **Transaction Payment Options** – Retrieve available payment methods for a transaction (mobile, bank transfer, credit card, etc.).  
3. **Merchant Operations** – Merchant-level services such as `getServices` to discover configured service IDs.  
4. **xPay Payments** – Execute xPay transactions and check company balance.  
5. **Super Wallet** – Wallet-based flows: create account, add card, get subscription token, pull account, customer charge token, recurrent charges, list transactions, delete card. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Navigation tree (key links): [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

- Transaction Operations  
  - Create Token (POST)  
  - Verify Transaction Token (POST)  
  - Refund Token (POST)  
  - Cancel Token (POST)  
  - Update Token (POST)  
  - Email to Token (POST)  
  - Verify xPay (POST)  
  - mVisa QR Code (POST)  

- Transaction Payment Options  
  - Get Mobile Payment Options (POST)  
  - Charge Token Auth (POST)  
  - Charge Token Bank Transfer (POST)  
  - Get Bank Transfer Options (POST)  
  - Charge Token Credit Card (POST)  
  - Charge Token Mobile (POST)  
  - Company Mobile Payment Options (POST)  

- Merchant Operations  
  - Get Services (POST)  

- xPay Payments  
  - Execute xPay (POST)  
  - Get Balance (POST)  

- Super Wallet  
  - Super Wallet / Create Account (POST)  
  - Super Wallet / Add Card (POST)  
  - Super Wallet / Get Subscription Token (POST)  
  - Super Wallet / Pull Account (POST)  
  - Super Wallet / Customer Charge Token (POST)  
  - Super Wallet / Charge Token Recurrent (POST)  
  - Super Wallet / Get Transactions (POST)  
  - Super Wallet / Delete Card (POST) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Typical Payment Flow
--------------------

A standard DPO Pay integration with V6 works as follows: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

1. **Create a payment token**  
   - Use Transaction Operations → `createToken`.  
2. **Retrieve available payment methods**  
   - Use Transaction Payment Options (e.g. mobile, card, bank-transfer options).  
3. **Send the customer through the payment experience**  
   - Redirect to hosted page or invoke the appropriate `chargeToken*` operation.  
4. **Process the transaction result**  
   - Handle callbacks, verify token, and update your order/subscription.  
5. **Extend with xPay or Super Wallet as needed**  
   - xPay for internal allocations/payouts.  
   - Super Wallet for stored cards and recurring payments. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Where to Start
--------------

For new integrations, start with: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

- **Transaction Operations → Create Token**  
  `createToken` is the entry point for most payment flows and underpins the rest of the operations. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Base URLs
---------

Use the following base URLs for all V6 requests: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

- **Sandbox:**  
  `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6/`  

- **Production:**  
  `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6/` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Related Documentation Sections
------------------------------

From this overview you can navigate to: [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

- Quick Start Guide  
- Sandbox & Test Credentials  
- All Transaction Operations endpoints  
- All Transaction Payment Options endpoints  
- Merchant Operations (`getServices`)  
- xPay Payments (Execute xPay, Get Balance)  
- Super Wallet endpoints  
- Plugins and platform-specific integrations (Shopify, WooCommerce, etc.) [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Here’s the “Create Token (Transaction Operations)” reference summary in a clean form. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)

***

Create Token (Transaction Operations, v6)
=========================================

Purpose  
Create a **payment token** for a new transaction. This token is then used to redirect the customer to pay (hosted page) or to charge via specific payment-option calls (card, mobile, bank transfer, etc.). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)

Endpoint & Method  
- Base URL (sandbox): `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6/`  
- Base URL (live): `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6/`  
- Method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Note: In docs you may see a logical path label like `/transaction-operations-create-token`, but in practice you post to `/API/v6/` with `<Request>createToken</Request>` in the XML. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)

High-level flow using createToken  
1. Your backend calls `createToken` with transaction + customer details.  
2. DPO returns a `TransToken` (transaction token).  
3. You either:  
   - Redirect the customer to the hosted payment page, or  
   - Use the token with `chargeToken*` APIs (card/mobile/bank transfer).  
4. You receive callbacks and/or call `verifyToken` later to confirm final status. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)

This page (in the ReadMe UI) mainly wires the **API reference entry** to the underlying v6 base endpoint and shows standard response shells (`200`, `400`, `401`) and code examples; the full business-level field list and examples live under the general “Create Token” docs at `/developers/create-token` you’ve already been using. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)

Here’s a concise summary of **Verify Transaction Token (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_transaction_token)

***

Verify Transaction Token (v6)
=============================

Purpose  
Verify the status/details of an existing **transaction token** you previously created with `createToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_transaction_token)

Endpoint & Method  
- Base URL (sandbox): `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Base URL (live): `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs path label: `/transaction-operations-verify-transaction-token` (logical only; real calls still go to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_transaction_token)

Usage in your flow  
- Call this after redirect/callback (or on demand) to confirm final transaction status for a given `TransToken`.  
- Typical responses:  
  - `200` – successful verification (valid request).  
  - `400` – bad request (e.g., malformed XML/params).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_transaction_token)

If you want, I can next:  
- Draft a sample XML request/response shape for verification, aligned with your existing `createToken` XML. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Here’s a concise summary of **Refund Token (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_refund_token)

***

Refund Token (v6)
=================

Purpose  
Refund an existing **transaction** using its `TransToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_refund_token)

Endpoint & Method  
- Base URL (sandbox): `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Base URL (live): `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-operations-refund-token` (logical only; real calls still go to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_refund_token)

Behavior & Responses  
- Use when you need to **refund or void** a completed/authorized transaction, as described in the more general “Refund / Void (v6)” docs. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_refund_token)
- Response codes:  
  - `200` – refund request accepted/processed.  
  - `400` – bad request (invalid or missing params/XML).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_refund_token)

If you want, I can help you next by drafting sample XML for `refundToken` that fits your existing `createToken` / `verifyToken` flow. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)


Here’s a concise summary of **Cancel Token (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_cancel_token)

***

Cancel Token (v6)
=================

Purpose  
Cancel a **pending/authorized transaction** using its `TransToken`, before or instead of capturing/charging it. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_cancel_token)

Endpoint & Method  
- Base URL (sandbox): `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Base URL (live): `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-operations-cancel-token` (logical; actual calls still go to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_cancel_token)

Behavior & Responses  
- Use when you want to **void/cancel** a token so it can no longer be used for payment. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_cancel_token)
- Response status codes:  
  - `200` – cancellation accepted/processed.  
  - `400` – bad request (invalid XML/params).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_cancel_token)

If you’d like, I can now put together a small table comparing **Verify / Refund / Cancel / Update Token** so you can wire clean service methods in your backend. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)

Here’s a concise summary of **Update Token (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_update_token)

***

### Update Token (v6)

**Purpose**  
Update an existing **transaction token’s details** (for example, changing amount, description, or selected service fields allowed by DPO) before the transaction is finalized. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_update_token)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-operations-update-token` (logical label only; real calls still go to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_update_token)

**Responses**  
- `200` – Successful update.  
- `400` – Bad request (invalid/missing parameters or malformed XML).  
- `401` – Authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_update_token)

***

### Quick comparison (Verify vs Refund vs Cancel vs Update)

| Operation | Main use | Typical timing | Effect on token/transaction |
|----------|----------|----------------|-----------------------------|
| Verify Token | Check current status & details | After payment / on-demand | Read-only status lookup | 
| Refund Token | Return funds for a completed charge | After successful payment | Creates a refund / voids settlement | 
| Cancel Token | Void a pending token | Before payment or capture | Token becomes unusable | 
| Update Token | Change details of an existing token | Before final payment | Edits allowed fields on the token | 

 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_transaction_token)

If you tell me your exact Odoo/Node flow (create → hosted page vs direct charge), I can map these four operations into clear service methods for your integration.

Here’s a concise summary of **Email to Token (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_email_to_token)

***

### Email to Token (v6)

**Purpose**  
Send a **payment link by email** to the customer for an existing, tokenized transaction (`TransToken`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_email_to_token)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-operations-email-to-token` (logical only; actual calls still go to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_email_to_token)

**Behavior & Responses**  
- Use when you want DPO to send the **hosted checkout link** directly to the customer’s email instead of (or in addition to) redirecting them yourself. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_email_to_token)
- Response codes:  
  - `200` – email dispatch accepted.  
  - `400` – bad request (invalid/missing params/XML).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_email_to_token)

If you want, I can draft a reusable helper around your existing `createToken` flow so you can optionally trigger this “email payment link” step from Odoo/Node.

Here’s a concise summary of **Verify xPay (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_xpay)

***

### Verify xPay (v6)

**Purpose**  
Check / verify the **status of an xPay request** previously initiated via the xPay APIs. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_xpay)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-operations-verify-xpay` (logical label only; real calls typically post to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_xpay)

**Responses**  
- `200` – Successful verification response.  
- `400` – Bad request (invalid or missing fields / malformed XML).  
- `401` – Authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_xpay)

Use this when you’re working with **xPay Payments** (internal balance / payout-type flows) and need to confirm the final state of a specific xPay operation, analogous to how you use **Verify Transaction Token** for standard card/mobile transactions. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Here’s a concise summary of **mVisa QR Code (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_mvisa_qr_code)

***

### mVisa QR Code (v6)

**Purpose**  
Create an **mVisa QR code** for an existing transaction so a customer can scan and pay via their Visa-supported banking app. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_mvisa_qr_code)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-operations-mvisa-qr-code` (logical; real calls still go to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_mvisa_qr_code)

**Behavior & Responses**  
- You call this after creating a token (or with sufficient transaction details) to obtain QR data for mVisa payment. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_mvisa_qr_code)
- Response codes:  
  - `200` – QR creation successful (QR payload / reference returned).  
  - `400` – bad request (invalid/missing fields, malformed XML).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_mvisa_qr_code)

If you tell me your flow (web vs POS vs PDF invoice), I can outline how to generate the mVisa QR, embed it (e.g., as PNG/SVG), and still keep your existing `createToken` / `verifyToken` logic consistent. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)

Here’s a concise summary of **Get Mobile Payment Options (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_mobile_payment_options)

### Get Mobile Payment Options (v6)

**Purpose**  
Retrieve **available mobile payment methods** (e.g., mobile money, wallets) for a given transaction token (`TransToken`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_mobile_payment_options)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-payment-options-get-mobile-payment-options` (logical; real calls typically still go to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_mobile_payment_options)

**Behavior & Responses**  
- Used right after `createToken` when you want to **offer mobile options in your own UI** instead of just sending the user to the hosted page. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)
- Response codes:  
  - `200` – success: list of mobile payment options for that token.  
  - `400` – bad request (invalid/missing fields or malformed XML).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_mobile_payment_options)

If you want, I can next sketch a minimal end‑to‑end flow for:  
`createToken → getMobilePaymentOptions → chargeTokenMobile → verifyToken` tailored to your Node/Odoo integration. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Here’s a concise summary of **Charge Token Auth (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_auth)

### Charge Token Auth (v6)

**Purpose**  
Perform an **authorization-only charge** on an existing transaction token (`TransToken`) rather than a full capture, so you can capture/settle later (depending on DPO’s config for your account). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_auth)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-payment-options-charge-token-auth` (logical label; real calls generally post to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_auth)

**Behavior & Responses**  
- Used after `createToken` (and typically after selecting a specific payment option) when you want to **authorize** the amount on the customer’s funding source. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)
- Response codes:  
  - `200` – successful authorization response.  
  - `400` – bad request (missing/invalid fields, malformed XML).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_auth)

If you tell me whether you actually need separate **auth + capture** semantics (vs straight sale), I can map which of DPO’s `chargeToken*` calls you should wire into your Node/Odoo services and where `Charge Token Auth` fits in that flow. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_mobile_payment_options)

Here’s a concise summary of **Charge Token — Bank Transfer (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_bank_transfer)

### Charge Token — Bank Transfer (v6)

**Purpose**  
Charge an existing **transaction token** (`TransToken`) using a **bank transfer** payment option, after you’ve obtained bank-transfer options for that token. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_bank_transfer)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-payment-options-charge-token-bank-transfer` (logical; v6 requests are generally still posted to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_bank_transfer)

**Behavior & Responses**  
- Used after `createToken` and typically after `Get Bank Transfer Options`, when the customer chooses a specific bank transfer method and you want DPO to process that charge. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)
- Response codes:  
  - `200` – successful bank-transfer charge response.  
  - `400` – bad request (invalid/missing params, malformed XML).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_bank_transfer)

If you’d like, I can next outline the full bank‑transfer flow for your integration:

`createToken → getBankTransferOptions → chargeTokenBankTransfer → verifyToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Here’s a concise summary of **Get Bank Transfer Options (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_bank_transfer_options)

### Get Bank Transfer Options (v6)

**Purpose**  
Retrieve the list of **available bank transfer methods** for a given transaction token, so you can present specific bank-transfer choices in your own UI. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_bank_transfer_options)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-payment-options-get-bank-transfer-options` (logical; actual v6 calls are generally posted to `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_bank_transfer_options)

**Behavior & Responses**  
- Used after `createToken` when the customer wants to pay via **bank transfer** and you need to know which concrete options (banks / schemes) DPO exposes for that token. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)
- Typical flow: `createToken → getBankTransferOptions → chargeTokenBankTransfer → verifyToken`. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_bank_transfer)
- Response codes:  
  - `200` – success, options returned.  
  - `400` – bad request (invalid/missing params, malformed XML).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_bank_transfer_options)


### Charge Token — Credit Card (v6)

**Purpose**  
Charge an existing **transaction token** by taking **direct card (PAN) details** in your own UI and sending them to DPO for processing. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_credit_card)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/transaction-payment-options-charge-token-credit-card` (logical path; requests are still posted to `/API/v6/` in practice). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_credit_card)

**Behavior & Responses**  
- Used after `createToken` when you want to **collect card data yourself** instead of using DPO’s hosted checkout. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)
- Response codes:  
  - `200` – card charge processed (success/decline info in body).  
  - `400` – bad request (invalid/missing params, malformed XML).  
  - `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_charge_token_credit_card)

Because this involves handling raw card data, it implies **PCI DSS responsibilities on your side**; if you’d like, I can help you compare using this vs the safer **hosted page** or **Super Wallet** tokenisation flows for your integration. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

- Content-Type: `application/xml`

**Behavior & Responses**  
- Used after `createToken` (often after `Get Mobile Payment Options`) when the customer chooses a **mobile money** method and you want DPO to initiate that mobile charge. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)
- Response codes:  
  - `200` – successful mobile charge response.  
  - `400` – bad request (invalid/missing fields, malformed XML).

### Company Mobile Payment Options (v6)

**Purpose**  
List all **mobile payment options enabled at company level** (for your DPO merchant account), independent of a specific transaction token. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_company_mobile_payment_options)

This is useful to:  
- Discover which **mobile money providers** (MTN, Airtel, etc. depending on config) are globally available for your company.  
- Pre‑configure your UI (badges, filters) before you hit token‑specific endpoints like **Get Mobile Payment Options**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_get_mobile_payment_options)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path shown as:  
  `/transaction-payment-options-company-mobile-payment-options`  
  but v6 calls are typically still sent as `POST` to the base endpoint. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_company_mobile_payment_options)

**Responses**  
- `200` – success, company‑level mobile options returned.  
- `400` – bad request.  
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_payment_options_company_mobile_payment_options)

***

### How it fits with the other “mobile” endpoints

| Endpoint                               | Scope                         | Typical use in flow                                      |
|----------------------------------------|------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------|
| Company Mobile Payment Options         | Company-wide config          | Know which mobile methods your account supports at all. |
| Get Mobile Payment Options             | Specific `TransToken`        | Filter methods actually valid for that transaction.     |
| Charge Token Mobile                    | Specific `TransToken` + choice | Initiate the selected mobile money payment.            |

 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Here’s a concise summary of **Get Services (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/merchant_operations_get_services)

### Get Services (Merchant Operations, v6)

**Purpose**  
List the **services configured for your DPO company account** (service IDs and related metadata), so you know which `ServiceID` values you can safely use in `createToken` and other operations. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/merchant_operations_get_services)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/merchant-operations-get-services` (logical; real v6 calls are typically posted to the base `/API/v6` endpoint). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/merchant_operations_get_services)

**Responses**  
- `200` – successful response with the list of available services for the company.  
- `400` – bad request.  
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/merchant_operations_get_services)

**How it fits your flow**  
Typical pattern is:  
`getServices → pick appropriate ServiceID for product/brand → createToken (with that ServiceID) → then use payment-option / charge / verify flows as needed.` [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/dpo-pay-api-v6)

Here’s a concise summary of **Execute xPay (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_execute_xpay)

### Execute xPay (v6)

**Purpose**  
Run an **xPay allocation** from your DPO company balance, according to the xPay configuration on your account (e.g., payouts, internal transfers, or balances managed via DPO). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_execute_xpay)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/xpay-payments-execute-xpay` (logical; DPO notes that v6 requests are “typically sent as POST to the base endpoint `/API/v6/`”). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_execute_xpay)

**Responses**  
- `200` – successful xPay execution response.  
- `400` – bad request (bad/missing params, malformed XML).  
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_execute_xpay)

**How it fits with Verify xPay and Get Balance**

| Endpoint        | Role in xPay flow                       |
|-----------------|------------------------------------------|
| Execute xPay    | Initiate an xPay allocation / transfer. |
| Verify xPay     | Check status of a specific xPay request. |
| Get Balance     | Check company xPay balance.             |

 [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_xpay)

Here’s a concise summary of **Get Balance (xPay, v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_get_balance)

### Get Balance (xPay – v6)

**Purpose**  
Retrieve your **company’s xPay balance for a specific currency**, so you know how much is available for xPay allocations/payouts. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_get_balance)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/xpay-payments-get-balance` (logical label; DPO notes that v6 requests are “typically sent as POST to the base endpoint `/API/v6/`”). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_get_balance)

**Responses**  
- `200` – successful balance response (includes balance for requested currency).  
- `400` – bad request (invalid/missing params or malformed XML).  
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_get_balance)

**Where it fits in xPay flows**

Typical xPay sequence:

1. **Get Balance** – check that sufficient funds exist for intended allocations. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_get_balance)
2. **Execute xPay** – perform the allocation/payout. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/xpay_payments_execute_xpay)
3. **Verify xPay** – confirm final status of that xPay request. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_verify_xpay)

Here’s a concise summary of **Super Wallet / Create Account (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)

### Super Wallet / Create Account (v6)

**Purpose**  
Create a **Super Wallet account** for a customer, optionally performing a small **$0.15 authorization** to verify the card. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)

This is the entry point for DPO’s **Super Wallet / tokenisation / recurring payments** flows. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/super-wallet-super-wallet-create-account` (logical label; DPO notes v6 requests are “typically sent as POST to the base endpoint `/API/v6/`”). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)

**Responses**  
- `200` – wallet account successfully created (and card verified, if applicable).  
- `400` – bad request (invalid/missing fields, malformed XML).  
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)

**How it fits in Super Wallet flows**

Typical Super Wallet lifecycle:

1. **Create Account** – set up the customer’s wallet record (this API). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
2. **Add Card** – attach payment card(s) to that wallet. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
3. **Get Subscription Token / Customer Charge Token / Charge Token Recurrent** – perform one‑off or recurring charges using stored tokens. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
4. **Pull Account / Get Transactions** – retrieve wallet details and history. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
5. **Delete Card** – remove stored cards. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)

Here’s a concise summary of **Super Wallet / Add Card (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_add_card)

***

### Super Wallet / Add Card (v6)

**Purpose**  
Add a **new payment card** to an **existing Super Wallet customer** so it can be used later for tokenised / recurring / one‑click payments. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_add_card)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/super-wallet-super-wallet-add-card` (logical label; DPO notes that v6 requests are typically sent as POST to the base `/API/v6/` endpoint). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_add_card)

**Responses**  
- `200` – card successfully added to the customer’s Super Wallet.  
- `400` – bad request (invalid/missing fields or malformed XML).  
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_add_card)

**How it fits in Super Wallet flows**

Typical sequence:

1. **Create Account** – create the Super Wallet customer. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
2. **Add Card** – attach one or more cards to that customer (this API). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_add_card)
3. Use **Get Subscription Token / Customer Charge Token / Charge Token Recurrent** to actually bill those stored cards. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_add_card)

Here’s a concise summary of **Super Wallet / Get Subscription Token (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)

### Super Wallet / Get Subscription Token (v6)

**Purpose**  
Fetch a customer’s **subscription token** and **customer token** using their **email or phone number**, so you can charge them later via Super Wallet recurring / tokenised flows. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/super-wallet-super-wallet-get-subscription-token` (logical; DPO notes v6 calls are “typically sent as POST to the base endpoint `/API/v6/`”). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)

**Responses**  
- `200` – successful, returns subscription/customer tokens for that email/phone. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)
- `400` – bad request (invalid/missing fields or malformed XML). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)

**How it fits the Super Wallet flow**

A typical recurring‑billing flow:

1. **Create Account** for the customer. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
2. **Add Card** to the wallet. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_add_card)
3. **Get Subscription Token** later by email/phone when you need to bill them (instead of storing tokens yourself). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)
4. Use that token with **Customer Charge Token / Charge Token Recurrent** to perform actual charges. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)

Here’s a concise summary of **Super Wallet / Pull Account (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_pull_account)

***

### Super Wallet / Pull Account (v6)

**Purpose**  
Retrieve a customer’s **saved payment options / subscription tokens** from Super Wallet, so you can see which stored cards/tokens are available to charge. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_pull_account)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/super-wallet-super-wallet-pull-account` (logical label; DPO notes v6 requests are “typically sent as POST to the base endpoint `/API/v6/`”). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_pull_account)

**Responses**  
- `200` – successful response with the customer’s saved payment options (subscription tokens). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_pull_account)
- `400` – bad request. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_pull_account)
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_pull_account)

**How it fits the Super Wallet flow**

You generally use this when you want to **inspect or display** what’s stored for a given customer before charging them:

1. Create Account / Add Card / store tokens. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
2. **Pull Account** – list saved payment options for that customer. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_pull_account)
3. Use **Customer Charge Token / Charge Token Recurrent** to bill one of those stored options. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_pull_account)

Here’s a concise summary of **Super Wallet / Customer Charge Token (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_customer_charge_token)

***

### Super Wallet / Customer Charge Token (v6)

**Purpose**  
Charge a customer using a **stored subscription token** (from Super Wallet) together with a **transaction token** (`TransToken`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_customer_charge_token)

This lets you bill a stored card without asking the customer for card details again, ideal for one‑click or recurring style payments. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path shown as:  
  `/super-wallet-super-wallet-customer-charge-token`  
  but DPO clarifies that v6 requests are **typically sent as POST to the base endpoint `/API/v6/`**, with this path being a *logical* label only. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_customer_charge_token)

**Responses**  
- `200` – successful charge response. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_customer_charge_token)
- `400` – bad request (invalid/missing params or malformed XML). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_customer_charge_token)
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_customer_charge_token)

**Where it sits in the Super Wallet flow**

A common pattern:

1. **Create Account** – create Super Wallet profile. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
2. **Add Card** – store card(s) for that customer. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_add_card)
3. **Get Subscription Token / Pull Account** – retrieve the customer/subscription token when you want to bill. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_pull_account)
4. **Customer Charge Token** – combine subscription token + `TransToken` to charge the stored card. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/transaction_operations_create_token)
5. Optionally use **Charge Token Recurrent** for scheduled recurring charges. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_customer_charge_token)

If you tell me your exact recurring / one‑click use case (e.g., monthly SaaS invoice in Odoo vs wallet inside your own app), I can lay out the minimal XML fields and call order you actually need from this Super Wallet set.

Here’s a concise summary of **Super Wallet / Charge Token Recurrent (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_charge_token_recurrent)

***

### Super Wallet / Charge Token Recurrent (v6)

**Purpose**  
Process a **recurring charge** using a customer’s **subscription token**, i.e., automated repeat billing via Super Wallet without re‑entering card details. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_charge_token_recurrent)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Docs label path: `/super-wallet-super-wallet-charge-token-recurrent` (logical label; DPO notes v6 requests are typically just `POST` to the base `/API/v6/` endpoint). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_charge_token_recurrent)

**Responses**  
- `200` – successful recurring charge response. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_charge_token_recurrent)
- `400` – bad request (invalid/missing params or malformed XML). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_charge_token_recurrent)
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_charge_token_recurrent)

**Where it fits in the Super Wallet lifecycle**

Typical recurring billing pattern:

1. **Create Account** → create wallet profile. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
2. **Add Card** → store card. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_add_card)
3. **Get Subscription Token / Pull Account** → retrieve subscription token for that customer. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_subscription_token)
4. **Charge Token Recurrent** → run scheduled/automatic charges using that subscription token (for each billing cycle). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_charge_token_recurrent)
5. Optionally use **Get Transactions** to review history and **Delete Card** to stop using that card. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_charge_token_recurrent)

Here’s a concise summary of **Super Wallet / Get Transactions (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_transactions)

***

### Super Wallet / Get Transactions (v6)

**Purpose**  
List **transactions for a given Super Wallet customer**, ordered from newest to oldest. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_transactions)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Logical docs path: `/super-wallet-super-wallet-get-transactions` (label only; v6 requests are typically just `POST` to the base `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_transactions)

**Responses**  
- `200` – successful, returns the customer’s transaction list (newest first). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_transactions)
- `400` – bad request (invalid/missing params, malformed XML). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_transactions)
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_get_transactions)

**Place in Super Wallet flows**  
Use this to **view or show history** for a wallet customer after you’ve been running charges via: Create Account, Add Card, Customer Charge Token, and Charge Token Recurrent. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)

Here’s a concise summary of **Super Wallet / Delete Card (v6)**. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_delete_card)

***

### Super Wallet / Delete Card (v6)

**Purpose**  
Delete a **stored card** from Super Wallet, identified by its **subscription token**, so it can no longer be used for tokenised or recurring payments. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_delete_card)

**Endpoint & Method**  
- Sandbox base: `https://secure1.sandbox.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- Live base: `https://secure1.directpay.online/API/v6`  
- HTTP method: `POST`  
- Content-Type: `application/xml`  
- Logical docs path: `/super-wallet-super-wallet-delete-card` (label only; v6 requests are typically just `POST` to the base `/API/v6/`). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_delete_card)

**Responses**  
- `200` – card deleted successfully. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_delete_card)
- `400` – bad request (invalid/missing params, malformed XML). [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_delete_card)
- `401` – authentication error. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_delete_card)

**Place in the Super Wallet lifecycle**

You typically use this when a customer wants to **remove a card on file** or you need to hard‑stop future recurring charges on that card:

- After using **Create Account**, **Add Card**, **Customer Charge Token**, and **Charge Token Recurrent**, call **Delete Card** with the subscription token for the specific card to remove it from the wallet. [docs.dpopay](https://docs.dpopay.com/dpo-pay-by-network/reference/super_wallet_super_wallet_create_account)
